Question:

[Image]


‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá [math]\vec{A}=3 \hat{i}+7 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-2 \hat{\mathrm{k}} ; \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}}=9 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-3 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\hat{\mathrm{k}}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{C}=\left(2 x y^{2}-4 z x\right) \hat{i}+\left(7 x^{3} y z^{2}+2 z x\right) \hat{j}-5 y^{2} z^{3} \hat{k}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ò. (‚Äì 1, 2, ‚Äì 2) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá C ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø Y ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶â‡ßé‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ùù∑ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º? ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ì‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\vec{A}=3 \hat{i}+7 \hat{j}-2 \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{1.5cm}\vec{B}=9 \hat{i}-3 \hat{j}+\hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£, [math]\theta = ?[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\hspace{1cm}\begin{array}{l}\vec{A}\cdot\vec{B}=AB\cos\theta\\\Rightarrow (3\hat{i}+7\hat{j}-2\hat{k})\cdot(9\hat{i}-3\hat{j}+\hat{k})=\sqrt{3^2+7^2+(-2)^2}.\sqrt{9^2(-3)^2+1^2}\cos\theta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{1cm}\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 27-21-2=\sqrt{9+49+4}\cdot\sqrt{81+9+1}\cos\theta\\\Rightarrow\cos\theta=\frac{4}{\sqrt{62}\cdot\sqrt{91}}\\\therefore\theta=86.94^{\circ}\\\end{array}[/math]
(‚Äì1, 2, ‚Äì 2) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{C}}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø[math]\begin{aligned}\overrightarrow{\mathrm{C}} & =\left\{2(-1) \cdot 2^{2}-4 \times 2(-1)\right\} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\left\{7(-1)^{3} 32(-2)^{2}+2(-2)\right. \ (-1)\} \hat{\mathrm{j}}-\left\{5 \times 2^{2} \cdot(-2)^{3}\right\} \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\& =-52 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+160 \hat{\mathrm{k}}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{C}}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø Y ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶â‡ßé‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£ [math]\theta'[/math]
 ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos \theta^{\prime}=\frac{-52}{\sqrt{(-52)^{2}+160^{2}}} \\\Rightarrow \theta^{\prime}=\cos ^{-1}\left(-\frac{52}{\sqrt{(-52)^{2}+160^{2}}}\right)=108^{\circ} \\\therefore \theta 
eq \theta^{\prime}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ( 1, 2, ‚àí 2 ) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{C}}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø Y ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶â‡ßé‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ [math]\theta[/math]
 ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ò ‡¶™‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá [math]\vec C[/math] ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec C=(-16,\,-52,\,160)[/math]. Y ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá [math]\cos\theta=\dfrac{C_y}{|\vec C|}=\dfrac{-52}{\sqrt{28560}}0[/math]. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º [math]\theta>\omega[/math] ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé C ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ Y ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶â‡ßé‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ [math]\omega[/math]-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º‡•§

Question #2 (ID: 395687)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: BoCPSC
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá [math]\vec{A}=\left(x^{2}+y z^{2}\right) \hat{i}+\left(y^{2}+z x^{2}\right) \hat{j}+\left(z^{2}+x y\right) \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§

Options:
‡¶ó. ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\vec{A}=\left(x^{2}+y z\right) \hat{i}+\left(y^{2}+z x\right) \hat{j}+\left(z^{2}+x y\right) \hat{k}[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏[math]\begin{aligned}
abla \cdot \vec{A} & =\left(\hat{i} \frac{\partial}{\partial x}+\hat{j} \frac{\partial}{\partial y}+\hat{k} \frac{\partial}{\partial z}\right) \cdot\left\{\left(\ddot{x}^{2}+y z\right) \hat{i}+\left(y^{2}+z x\right) \hat{j}+\left(z^{2}+x y\right) \hat{k}\right\} \\& =\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(x^{2}+y z\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(y^{2}+z x\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(z^{2}+x y\right) \\& =(2 x+2 y+2 z)\end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ [math](2 x+2 y+2 z)[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:
‡¶ó ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® [math]\nabla\cdot\vec{A}=\partial_x A_x+\partial_y A_y+\partial_z A_z[/math]‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\partial_x(x^2+yz^2)=2x,\ \partial_y(y^2+zx^2)=2y,\ \partial_z(z^2+xy)=2z[/math] ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤ [math]2x+2y+2z=2(x+y+z)[/math]‡•§

Question #3 (ID: 395688)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: BoCPSC
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá [math]\vec{A}=\left(x^{2}+y z^{2}\right) \hat{i}+\left(y^{2}+z x^{2}\right) \hat{j}+\left(z^{2}+x y\right) \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§

Options:
‡¶ò. ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\vec{A}=\left(x^{2}+y z\right) \hat{i}+\left(y^{2}+z x\right) \hat{j}+\left(z^{2}+x y\right) \hat{k}[/math]
‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤,[math]\begin{array}{l}
abla\times\vec{A}\quad\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i}&\hat{j}&\hat{\mathrm{k}}\\\frac{\partial}{\partial x}&\frac{\partial}{\partial y}&\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\\\left(x^2+yz\right)&\left(y^2+zx\right)&\left(z^2+xy\right)\end{array}\right|\ \\\ \ \ \ \ \ =\hat{i}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(z^2+xy\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(y^2+zx\right)\right\}-\hat{j}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(z^2+xy\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(x^2+yz\right)\right\}+\hat{k}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(y^2+zx\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(x^2+yz\right)\right\}\\\ \ \ \ \ \ =\hat{i}(x-x)-\hat{j}(y-y)+\hat{k}(z-z)\\\ \ \ \ \ \ =0\\\because
abla\times\vec{A}=0\\\end{array}[/math]
‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º [math]\nabla\times\vec{A}=(x-x^{2})\hat{i}+(2yz-y)\hat{j}+(2xz-z^{2})\hat{k}[/math]. ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ (‡¶Ö‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º), ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Question #4 (ID: 395689)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Narail Govt. Victoria College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{Q}=2 \mathrm{x} y^{4}-x^{2} \mathrm{z}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡•§

Options:
‡¶ó. (1, ‚àí 1, 1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá Q ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]Q=2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, [math]\operatorname{grad} Q=\vec{
abla} \cdot Q=\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right\} \cdot\left\{2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z\right\}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{2.5cm}\begin{array}{l}=\hat{i} \frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z\right)+\hat{j} \frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z\right)+\hat{k} \frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z\right) \\=\hat{i}\left(2 y^{4}-2 x z\right)+\hat{j}\left(8 x y^{3}-0\right)+\hat{k}\left(0-x^{2}\right) \\=\left(2 y^{4}-2 x z\right) \hat{i}+8 x y^{3} \hat{j}-x^{2} \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore(1,-1,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá Q ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü[math]\hspace{1.5cm}\begin{array}{l}=\left(2(-1)^{4}-2 \cdot 1 \cdot 1\right) \hat{i}+8(1)(-1)^{3} \hat{j}-(1)^{2} \hat{k} \\=0 \hat{i}-8 \hat{j}-\hat{k}=-8 \hat{j}-\hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶ó ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤ [math]\partial Q/\partial x=2y^{4}-2xz,\;\partial Q/\partial y=8xy^{3},\;\partial Q/\partial z=-x^{2}[/math]. [math](1,-1,1)[/math] ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla Q(1,-1,1)=(0,-8,-1)[/math] ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ [math]y^{4}=1,\;8xy^{3}=8\cdot1\cdot(-1)^{3}=-8,\; -x^{2}=-1[/math].

Question #5 (ID: 395690)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Narail Govt. Victoria College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{Q}=2 \mathrm{x} y^{4}-x^{2} \mathrm{z}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡•§

Options:
‡¶ò. ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßá, [math]\vec{\nabla} \mathrm{Q}[/math] ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‚Äò‡¶ó‚Äô ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l}\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{Q}=\left(2 y^{4}-2 x z\right) \hat{i}+8 x y^{3} \hat{j}-x^{2} \hat{k} \\\vec{
abla}=\hat{i} \frac{\partial}{\partial x}+\hat{j} \frac{\partial}{\partial y}+\hat{k} \frac{\partial}{\partial z}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\text { Curl }=\vec{
abla} \times \vec{Q}=0[/math]
 ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá,[math]\hspace{1.5cm}\begin{array}{l}\vec{
abla}\times\vec{Q}=\left(\hat{i}\frac{\partial}{\partial x}+\hat{j}\frac{\partial}{\partial y}+\hat{k}\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\right)\times\left\{\left(2y^4-2xz\right)\hat{i}+8xy^3\hat{j}-x^2k\right\}\\=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i}&\hat{j}&\hat{k}\\\frac{\partial}{\partial x}&\cdot\frac{\partial}{\partial y}&\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\\2y^4-2xz&,8xy^3&-x^2\end{array}\right|\\=\hat{i}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(-x)^2-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(8xy^3\right)\right\}+\hat{j}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2y^4-2xz\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(-x^2\right)\right\}+\hat{k}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(8xy^3\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(2y^4-2xz\right)\right\}\\=\hat{\mathrm{i}}(0-0)\hat{\mathrm{j}}(0-2\mathrm{x}+2\mathrm{x})+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(8\mathrm{y}^3-8\mathrm{y}^3+0\right)\\=\hat{\mathrm{i}}\cdot0+\hat{\mathrm{j}}\cdot0+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\cdot0=0\\\end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ [math]\vec{
abla} \times \vec{Q}=0[/math]
 ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec{
abla} \mathrm{Q}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá [math]\vec{\nabla}Q=(\partial_x Q,\partial_y Q,\partial_z Q)=(2y^4-2xz,\;8xy^3,\;-x^2)[/math] ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ [math]\nabla\times(\nabla Q)[/math] ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶ü‡¶ø [math]\partial_y(-x^2)-\partial_z(8xy^3)=0[/math], ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶ø [math]\partial_z(2y^4-2xz)-\partial_x(-x^2)=-2x-(-2x)=0[/math], ‡¶§‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶ø [math]\partial_x(8xy^3)-\partial_y(2y^4-2xz)=8y^3-8y^3=0[/math] ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\times(\nabla Q)=\mathbf{0}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{\nabla}Q[/math] ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§

Question:
[math]A=x^{2} y i-2 x z j+2 y z k[/math]‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]B=3 x^{2} y z+4 x y z+2 y z^{3}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ï‡•§

Options:
‡¶ó. Curl A ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø, ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶∞, [math]\vec{
abla}=\hat{i} \frac{\partial}{\partial x}+\hat{j} \frac{\partial}{\partial y}+[/math]
‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á, [math]\vec{A}=x^{2} y \hat{i}-2 x z \hat{j}+2 y z \hat{k}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, [math]\operatorname{Curl} \vec{A}=\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{2.3cm}\begin{array}{l}=\left(\hat{i}\frac{\partial}{\partial x}+\hat{j}\frac{\partial}{\partial y}+\hat{k}\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\right)\times\left(x^2y\hat{i}-2xz\hat{j}+2yz\hat{k}\right)\\=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i}&\hat{j}&\hat{k}\\\frac{\partial}{\partial x}&\frac{\partial}{\partial y}&\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\\x^2y&-2xz&2yz\end{array}\right|\\=\hat{i}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(2yz)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(-2xz)\right\}-\hat{j}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(2yz)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(x^2y\right)\right\}\hat{k}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(-2xz)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(x^2y\right)\right\}\\=\hat{\mathrm{i}}(2\mathrm{z}+2\mathrm{x})-\hat{\mathrm{j}}(0-0)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}(-2\mathrm{z}-\mathrm{x})\\=2(z+x)\hat{i}-\left(2z-x^2\right)\hat{k}\\\end{array}[/math]
‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßá‡ßü [math]\operatorname{curl} A=2(z+x) \hat{i}-\left(2 z-x^{2}\right) \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶ó [math]\nabla\times A[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÇ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ [math](\partial_y A_z-\partial_z A_y)\mathbf{i}-(\partial_x A_z-\partial_z A_x)\mathbf{j}+(\partial_x A_y-\partial_y A_x)\mathbf{k}[/math] ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø; ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\partial_y A_z=2z,\ \partial_z A_y=-2x,\ \partial_x A_z=0,\ \partial_z A_x=0,\ \partial_x A_y=-2z,\ \partial_y A_x=x^2[/math]. ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\times A=2(x+z)\mathbf{i}- (x^2+2z)\mathbf{k}[/math] (j ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø).

Question:

Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶∞, [math]\vec{
abla}=\hat{i} \frac{\partial}{\partial x}+\hat{j} \frac{\partial}{\partial y}+\hat{k} \frac{\partial}{\partial z}[/math]
‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, [math]B=3 x^{2} y z+4 x y^{2} z+2 y z^{3}[/math]
‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ B ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§[math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \operatorname{grad} B & =\vec{
abla} B \\& =\left(\hat{i} \frac{\partial}{\partial x}+\hat{j} \frac{\partial}{\partial y}+\hat{k} \frac{\partial}{\partial z}\right)\left(3 x^{2} y z+4 x y z+2 y z^{3}\right) \\& =\hat{i}(6 x y z+4 y z)+\hat{j}\left(3 x^{2} z+4 x z+2 z^{3}\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(3 \mathrm{x}^{2} \mathrm{y}+4 x y+6 y z^{2}\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{2.5cm}[/math]
 -‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞,‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã [math]\vec{A}=x^{2} y \hat{i}-2 x z \hat{j}+2 y z \hat{k}[/math]
‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ [math]\vec {A}[/math]
 ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡•§[math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \operatorname{div} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} & =\vec{
abla} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} \\& =\left(\hat{\mathrm{i}} \frac{\partial}{\partial x}+\hat{\mathrm{j}} \frac{\partial}{\partial y}+\hat{\mathrm{k}} \frac{\partial}{\partial z}\right)\left(x^{2} y \hat{i}-2 x z \hat{j}+2 y z \hat{k}\right) \\& =\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(x^{2} y\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(-2 x z)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(2 y z) \\& =2 x y+0+2 z\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{2cm}=2 x y+2 z[/math]
 ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ò ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé [math]\vec{F}=\nabla B[/math]; ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé [math]\phi=\nabla\cdot\vec{A}[/math], ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ì ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ï‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶â‡ßé‡¶∏ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Scholars Home, Sylhet

Question:
[math]\text { i. } \varphi=2 z-x^{3} y[/math]‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{a}=2 x^{3 \hat{i}}-3 \mathrm{yz \hat {j }}+\mathrm{x}^{2} \hat{k}[/math] [math]\text { ii. } \vec{F}=(\mathrm{x}+2 \mathrm{y}+\mathrm{az}) \hat{i}(\mathrm{bx}-3 \mathrm{y}-\mathrm{z}) \hat{j}+(4 \mathrm{x}+\mathrm{cv}+2 \mathrm{z}) \hat{k}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ó. (1, -1, 1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá, [math]\vec{a}, \vec{\varphi}[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá,[math]\hspace{.5cm}\begin{aligned}& \vec{a}=2 x^{2} \hat{i}-3 y z \hat{j}+x z^{2} \hat{k} \\\varphi & =2 z-x^{3} y \\\therefore \vec{
abla} \varphi= & \left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right)\left(2 z-x^{3} y\right) \\= & \hat{i} \frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(2 z-x^{3} y\right)+\hat{j} \frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(2 z-x^{3} y\right)+\hat{k} \frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2 z-x^{3} y\right) \\= & \hat{i}\left(-3 x^{2} y\right)+\hat{j}-\left(x^{3}\right)+\hat{k} \cdot 2 \\= & -3 x^{2} y \hat{i}-x^{3} \hat{j}+2 \hat{k} \\\therefore \vec{a} \cdot \vec{
abla} \varphi= & \left(2 x^{2} \hat{i}-3 y z \hat{j}+x z^{2} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left(-3 x^{2} y \hat{i}-x^{3} \hat{j}+2 \hat{k}\right) \\= & -6 x^{4} y+3 x^{3} y z+2 x z^{2}\end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, (1, ‚àí 1, 1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá[math]\hspace{.5cm}\begin{aligned}\vec{a} \cdot \vec{
abla} \varphi & =-6 \cdot 1^{4} \cdot(-1)+3 \cdot 1^{3} \cdot(-1) \cdot 1+2 \cdot 1 \cdot 1^{2} \\& =6-3+2=5\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ó ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá [math]\vec{a}[/math]-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá [math](x,y,z)=(1,-1,1)[/math] ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{a}=(2x^3)\hat{i}-3yz\hat{j}+x^2\hat{k}\Rightarrow \vec{a}(1,-1,1)=2\hat{i}+3\hat{j}+\hat{k}[/math]. ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ [math]\varphi=2z-x^3y[/math] ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla\varphi=(\partial\varphi/\partial x,\partial\varphi/\partial y,\partial\varphi/\partial z)=(-3x^2y,-x^3,2)[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\varphi(1,-1,1)=(3,-1,2)[/math].

Question #9 (ID: 395694)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Scholars Home, Sylhet

Question:
[math]\text { i. } \varphi=2 z-x^{3} y[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{a}=2 x^{3} \hat{i}-3 y \hat{z j}+x z^{2} \hat{k}[/math] [math]\text { ii. } \vec{F}=(x+2 y+a z) \hat{i}(b x-3 y-z) \hat{j}+(4 x+c v+2 z) \hat{k}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ò. a, b ‡¶ì c ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá F ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá? ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø, F ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, [math]\vec{
abla} \times \vec{F}=0[/math]
 ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore\vec{
abla}\times\vec{F}=0\\\Rightarrow \left|\begin{array}{c}\hat{i}\frac{\partial}{\partial x}x+2y+az\\\hat{j}\frac{\partial}{\partial y}bx-3y-z\\\hat{k}\frac{\partial}{\partial z}4x+cy+2z\end{array}\right|=0\\\Rightarrow \hat{i}(0+c+0+1)-\hat{j}(4+0+0-a)+\hat{k}(b-0-0-2-0)=0\\\Rightarrow \hat{i}(c+1)-\hat{j}(4-a)+\hat{k}(b-2)=0\end{array}[/math]
‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá, [math]\hat i,\hat j~ ‡¶ì ~\hat k[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ó ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá[math]\begin{array}{l}c+1=0\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -(4-a)=0\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ b-2=0\\\Rightarrow c=-1\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \Rightarrow a=4\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \Rightarrow b=2\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{a}=4, \mathrm{~b}=2 \text { ‡¶ì } \mathrm{c}=-1[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø F ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶ò ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá [math]v=y[/math] (‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡ßã) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla\times\vec F=0[/math]‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá, 
[math](\nabla\times\vec F)_x=\partial_yF_z-\partial_zF_y=c-(-1)=c+1, \quad (\nabla\times\vec F)_y=\partial_zF_x-\partial_xF_z=a-4, \quad (\nabla\times\vec F)_z=\partial_xF_y-\partial_yF_x=b-2.[math] 
‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá [math]a=4,\; b=2,\; c=-1[/math]‡•§

Question #10 (ID: 395676)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø [math]\vec{r}=b t^{2} \hat{i}+c t^{3} \hat{j}[/math] ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá b ‡¶ì c ‡¶ß‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ï‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ó ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ x ‡¶ì y ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá 45¬∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
( Answer : [math]\frac{2 b}{3 c}[/math]
 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, [math]\vec{r}=b^{2} \hat{i}+c^{3} \hat{j}[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\therefore \vec{v}=\frac{d \vec{r}}{d t}=2 b t \hat{i}+3 c t^{2} \hat{j}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® , [math]\tan 45^{\circ}=\frac{3 \mathrm{ct}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{bt}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]1=\frac{3 t^{2}}{2 b t}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]3 \mathrm{ct}^{2}=2 \mathrm{bt}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]3 c t=2 b[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{t}=\frac{2 \mathrm{~b}}{3 \mathrm{c}} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
[math]\vec v=\frac{d\vec r}{dt}=2bt\,\hat{i}+3ct^{2}\,\hat{j}[/math]. 45¬∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø [math]\tan\theta=1[/math] ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\dfrac{3ct^{2}}{2bt}=1[/math] (t‚â†0) ‡¶π‡ßü; ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá [math]t=\dfrac{2b}{3c}[/math]. t=0 ‡¶è ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶®‡ßü‡•§

Question #11 (ID: 395677)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ [math]\vec{r}=4 x^{2} t^{3} \hat{i}+2 y^{2} t^{2} \hat{j}[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ó ‡¶ì ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
( Answer : [math]12 x^{2} t^{2} \hat{i}+4 y^{2} t \hat{j}[/math]
 , [math]24 x^{2} t \hat{i}+4 y^{2} \hat{j}[/math]
 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£, [math]\vec{r}=4 x^{2} t^{3} \hat{i}+2 y^{2} t^{2} \hat{j}[/math]
‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ó, [math]\vec{\mathrm{v}}=?[/math]
‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶£, [math]\vec{a}=\text { ? }[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ó, [math]\vec{v}=\frac{d \vec{r}}{\mathrm{dt}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{d}{d t}\left(4 x^{2} t^{3} \hat{i}+2 y^{2} t^{2} \hat{j}\right)[/math]
 [math]\vec{v}=12 x^{2} t^{2} \hat{i}+4 y^{2} t \hat{j} \text { (Ans) }[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶£, [math]\vec{a}=\frac{d \vec{v}}{d t}=\frac{d}{d t}\left(12 x^{2} t^{2} \hat{i}+4 y^{2} t \hat{j}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \vec{\mathrm{a}}=24 \mathrm{x}^{2} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+4 \mathrm{y}^{2} \hat{\mathrm{j}} \text { (Ans) }[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®:
‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ó: [math]\vec{v}=\frac{d\vec{r}}{dt}=12x^{2}t^{2}\,\hat{i}+4y^{2}t\,\hat{j}[/math].  
‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶£: [math]\vec{a}=\frac{d\vec{v}}{dt}=24x^{2}t\,\hat{i}+4y^{2}\,\hat{j}[/math].

‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]x[/math] ‡¶ì [math]y[/math] ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ï ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá [math]t[/math] ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶™‡ßÉ‡¶•‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]t^{n}[/math]-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ [math]n t^{n-1}[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

Question #12 (ID: 395678)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Dhaka Residential Model College, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ [math]\varphi=2 x^{2} y^{2} z^{2}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ [math]\mathrm{F}=x^{2} y \mathrm{il}-2 x y z \mathrm{x}+2 \mathrm{yzk}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ó. ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ div grad [math]\varphi[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\varphi=2 x^{2} y^{2} z^{4}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \operatorname{grad} \varphi=
abla \phi=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}} \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{z}} \hat{\mathrm{k}}\right)\left(2 \mathrm{x}^{2} \mathrm{y}^{2} \mathrm{z}^{4}\right) \\\qquad \qquad=2 y^{2} z^{4}(2 x) \hat{i}+2 x^{2} z^{4}(2 y) \hat{j}+2 x^{2} y^{2}\left(4 z^{3}\right) \hat{k} \\\therefore \operatorname{grad} \phi=4 x y^{2} z^{4} \hat{i}+4 x^{2} y z^{4} \hat{j}+8 x^{2} y^{2} z^{3} \hat{k} \\\therefore \operatorname{div} \operatorname{grad} \varphi=\vec{
abla} \cdot \operatorname{grad} \varphi \\\qquad \qquad=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left(4 x y^{2} z^{4} \hat{i}+4 x^{2} y z^{4} \hat{j}+8 x^{2} y^{2} z^{3} \hat{k}\right) \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}& =4 y^{2} z^{4}(1)+4 x^{2} z^{4}(1)+8 x^{2} y^{2}\left(3 z^{2}\right) \\\therefore \operatorname{div} \operatorname{grad} \varphi & =4 y^{2} z^{4}+4 x^{2} z^{4}+24 x^{2} y^{2} z^{2}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ó div grad ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤ [math]\nabla^2\varphi[/math]‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\varphi=2x^2y^2z^2[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\partial\varphi/\partial x=4xy^2z^2[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\partial^2\varphi/\partial x^2=4y^2z^2[/math] (‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá [math]4x^2z^2[/math] ‡¶ì [math]4x^2y^2[/math] ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü)‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç [math]\nabla\cdot\nabla\varphi=\nabla^2\varphi=4\big(x^2y^2+x^2z^2+y^2z^2\big)[/math]‡•§

Question #13 (ID: 395679)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Dhaka Residential Model College, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ [math]\varphi=2 x^{2} y^{2} z^{2}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ [math]\mathrm{F}=x^{2} y i-2 x y z j+2 y z k[/math]

‡¶ò, (1, - 1, 1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá Curl F, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶ì‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\vec{F}=x^{2} y \hat{i}-2 x y z \hat{j}+2 y z \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \text { Curl } \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}=\vec{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}} \\=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\\frac{\partial}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\x^{2} y & -2 x y z & 2 y z\end{array}\right| \\=\hat{i}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(2 y z)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(-2 x y z)\right\}-\hat{j}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(2 y z)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(x^{2} y\right)\right\} +\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}}(-2 \mathrm{xyz})-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(\mathrm{x}^{2} \mathrm{y}\right)\right\} \\=\hat{\mathrm{i}}\{2 \mathrm{z}+2 \mathrm{xy}\}-\hat{\mathrm{j}}\{0-0\}+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left\{-2 \mathrm{yz}-\mathrm{x}^{2}\right\} \\\therefore \operatorname{Curl} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}=(2 x y+2 z) \hat{\mathrm{i}}-\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(\mathrm{x}^{2}+2 \mathrm{yz}\right) \\\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, (1, ‚àí 1, 1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\text { Curl } \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}=(-2+2) \hat{\mathrm{i}}-(1-2) \hat{\mathrm{k}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \text { Curl } \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}=\hat{\mathrm{k}}[/math]
‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá, [math]\text { Curl } \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}[/math]
 ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ (z) ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡•§‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶è‡¶¨, (1, ‚àí 1, 1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\text { Curl } \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∞‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤ [math]\nabla\times F[/math]; ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla\times F=(2(xy+z),\;0,\;-x^{2}-2yz)[/math]. (1,-1,1)-‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla\times F(1,-1,1)=(0,0,1)[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ z-‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‚Äî ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡•§

Question #14 (ID: 395680)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Dhaka City College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\vec{A}=2 \hat{i}-\hat{j}+2 \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\vec{B}=2 \hat{i}+3 \hat{j}+\hat{k}[/math] ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{F}=x^{2} y \hat{i}+y^{2} z \hat{j}+z^{2} x \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶£‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

Options:
‡¶ò. (1, ‚àí 1, 1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{F}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶ì ‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞,[math]\hspace{1.5cm}\overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}=x^{2} y \hat{i}+y^{2} z \hat{j}+z^{2} x \hat{k}[/math]
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá, [math]\operatorname{Curl} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{V}}=\vec{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{V}}[/math]
‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç [math]\mathrm{Curl} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}=\overrightarrow{\mathrm{V}} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \times\left(x^{2} y \hat{i}+y^{2} z \hat{j}+z^{2} x \hat{k}\right) \\=\left|\begin{array}{lll}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\\frac{\partial}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\x^{2} y & y^{2} \cdot z & z^{2} x\end{array}\right| \\=\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(z^{2} x\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(y^{2} z\right)\right\} \hat{i}-\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(z^{2} x\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(x^{2} y\right)\right\} \hat{j}+\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(y^{2} z\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(x^{2} y\right)\right\} \hat{k} \\=\left(0-y^{2}\right) \hat{i}-\left(z^{2}-0\right) \hat{j}+\left(0-x^{2}\right) \hat{k} \\=-y^{2} \hat{i}-z^{2} \hat{j}-x^{2} \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, (1, ‚àí 1, 1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá[math]\begin{aligned}\text { Curl } \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}} & =-(-1)^{2} \hat{\mathrm{i}}-(1)^{2} \hat{\mathrm{j}}-(1)^{2} \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\& =-\hat{\mathrm{i}}-\hat{\mathrm{j}}-\hat{\mathrm{k}} \\& =-(\hat{\mathrm{i}}+\hat{\mathrm{j}}+\hat{\mathrm{k}}) \\\mid \text { Curl } \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}} \mid & =\sqrt{(-1)^{2}+(-1)^{2}+(-1)^{2}} \\& =\sqrt{3}\end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç (1, ‚àí 1, 1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ã‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶Æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‚àö3 ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ò [math]\nabla\times\vec{F}=(\partial_y(z^2x)-\partial_z(y^2z))\hat{i}-(\partial_x(z^2x)-\partial_z(x^2y))\hat{j}+(\partial_x(y^2z)-\partial_y(x^2y))\hat{k}=-y^2\hat{i}-z^2\hat{j}-x^2\hat{k}[/math]. ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ [math](1,-1,1)[/math]-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá [math](-1,-1,-1)[/math]. ‡¶ö‡ßÇ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ê ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® (rotational) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ (conservative) ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Question #15 (ID: 395681)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Feni Girls' Cadet College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ [math]\vec{A}=\left(6 \mathrm{xy}+z^{2}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-\mathrm{z}\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 \mathrm{x} z^{2}-\mathrm{y}\right) \hat{k}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ó. (1, -1, 1 ) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{A}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá,[math]\vec{A}=\left(6 x y+z^{2}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat{k}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, [math]\operatorname{div} \vec{A}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left\{\left(6 x y+z^{2}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat{k}\right\}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{2cm}\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(6 x y+z^{2}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3 x^{2}-z\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \\=6 y+0+6 x z=6 y+6 xz \end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, (1, ‚àí 1, 1 ) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\operatorname{div} \vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®[math]\hspace{1cm}=6 \times(-1)+6 \times 1 \times 1=-6+6=0[/math]
‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\operatorname{div} \vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ó ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\nabla\cdot\vec{A}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(6xy+z^2)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(3x^2-z)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(3xz^2-y)=6y+6xz[/math]. [math]x=1,\;y=-1,\;z=1[/math] ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá [math]6(-1)+6(1)(1)=0[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

Question #16 (ID: 395682)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Feni Girls' Cadet College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ [math]\vec{A}=\left(6 \mathrm{xy}+z^{2}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-\mathrm{z}\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 \mathrm{x} z^{2}-\mathrm{y}\right) \hat{k}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ò. [math]\vec{A}[/math] ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤? ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\vec{A}=\left(6 x y+z^{2}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\operatorname{curl} \vec{A}=
abla \times \vec{A}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \times\left\{\left(6 x y+z^{2}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat{k}\right\}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}curl\vec{A}=
abla\times\vec{A}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\hat{k}\right)\times\left\{\left(6xy+z^2\right)\hat{i}+\left(3x^2-z\right)\hat{j}+\left(3xz^2-y\right)\hat{k}\right\}\\\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{\mathrm{i}}&\hat{\mathrm{j}}&\hat{\mathrm{k}}\\\frac{\partial}{\partial\mathrm{x}}&\frac{\partial}{\partial y}&\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\\\left(6xy+z^2\right)&\left(3\mathrm{x}^2-z\right)&\left(3xz^2-y\right)\end{array}\right|\\\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3xz^2-\mathrm{y}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(3x^2-z\right)\right\}+\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(6xy+z^2\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3xz^2-y\right)\right\}+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial\mathrm{x}}\left(3\mathrm{x}^2-\mathrm{z}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(6xy+z^2\right)\right\}\\\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\hat{i}(-1+1)+\hat{j}\left(2\cdot z-3z^2\right)+\hat{k}(6x-6x)=\left(2z-3z^2\right)\hat{j}\\\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\operatorname{curl} \vec{A} 
eq 0[/math]
‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø A ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶ò ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla\times\vec A=(\partial_y A_z-\partial_z A_y)\hat i+(\partial_z A_x-\partial_x A_z)\hat j+(\partial_x A_y-\partial_y A_x)\hat k[/math] ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\partial_y A_z=-1,\ \partial_z A_y=-1[/math], [math]\partial_z A_x=2z,\ \partial_x A_z=3z^2[/math], [math]\partial_x A_y=6x,\ \partial_y A_x=6x[/math]. ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla\times\vec A=(2z-3z^2)\hat j[/math], ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡ßü‡•§

Question:
‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßá [math]\vec{A}=2 \hat{i}-\hat{j}+3 \hat{k}[/math]‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{B}=\hat{i}+2 \hat{j}-4 \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ [math]\left(6 x^{2} y-z^{3}\right) i+2 x^{3} \hat{j}-3 x z^{2} \hat{k}[/math] ‡•§

Options:
‡¶ò. ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ [math]\vec P[/math] ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤? ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‚Äç‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø, ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶∞, [math]\vec{
abla}=\hat{\mathrm{i}} \frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}}+\hat{\mathrm{j}} \frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}}+\hat{\mathrm{k}} \frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{z}}[/math]
‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{p}}=\left(\hat{\mathrm{i}} \frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}}+\hat{\mathrm{j}} \frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}}+\hat{\mathrm{k}} \frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{z}}\right) \cdot\left(6 \mathrm{x}^{2} \mathrm{y}-\mathrm{z}^{3}\right) \hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 \mathrm{x}^{3} \hat{\mathrm{j}}-3 \mathrm{xz} \mathrm{z}^{2} \hat{\mathrm{k}}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{2.3cm}\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(6 x^{2} y-z^{3}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(2 x^{3}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(-3 x z^{2}\right) \\=12 x y+0-6 x z \\=12 x y-6 x z\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{P}} 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \overrightarrow{\mathrm{P}}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡•§‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞, [math]\operatorname{curl} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{P}}=\vec{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{P}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\left(\hat{i}\frac{\partial}{\partial x}+\hat{j}\frac{\partial}{\partial y}+\hat{k}\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\right)\times\left\{\left(6x^2y-z^3\right)\hat{i}+2x^3\hat{j}-3xz^2\hat{k}\right\}\\=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{\mathrm{i}}&\cdot\hat{\mathrm{j}}&\hat{\mathrm{k}}\\\frac{\partial}{\partial x}&\frac{\partial}{\partial y}&\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\\\left(6x^2y-z^3\right)&2\mathrm{x}^3&-3xz^2\end{array}\right|\\=\hat{i}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(-3xz^2\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2x^3\right)\right\}+\hat{j}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(6x^2y-z^3\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(-3xz^2\right)\right\}+\hat{k}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(2x^3\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(6x^2y-z^3\right)\right\}\\=\hat{\mathrm{i}}(0-0)+\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(-3z^2+3z^2\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(6\mathrm{x}^2-6\mathrm{x}^2\right)\\=0+0+0=0\\\end{array}[/math]
‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á,[math]\hspace{1cm}\operatorname{curl} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{P}}=\vec{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{P}}=0[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø, [math]\vec{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{P}}=0[/math]
 ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡ß∑‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶è‡¶¨, ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ò ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü: [math]\nabla\cdot\vec P=\partial_x(6x^2y-z^3)+\partial_y(2x^3)+\partial_z(-3xz^2)=12xy+0-6xz=6x(2y-z)[/math], ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡ßü, ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ì ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü: [math]\partial_yP_z-\partial_zP_y=0,\quad \partial_zP_x-\partial_xP_z=-3z^2-(-3z^2)=0,\quad \partial_xP_y-\partial_yP_x=6x^2-6x^2=0[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\times\vec P=\mathbf{0}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§

Question #18 (ID: 395684)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Barisal Cadet College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø [math]\vec{A}=\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-2 z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x y z+x^{2} y\right) \hat{k}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ó. ‚õõ. (‚õõ x A) = 0 ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨? ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ì‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\vec{A}=\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-2 z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x y z+x^{2} y\right) \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\vec{
abla}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\hat{k}\\\therefore\vec{
abla}\times\vec{A}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{\mathrm{i}}&\hat{\mathrm{j}}&\hat{\mathrm{k}}\\\frac{\partial}{\partial x}&\frac{\partial}{\partial y}&\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\\\left(6xy+z^3\right)&\left(3x^2-2z\right)&\left(3xyz+x^2y\right)\end{array}\right|\\=\left[\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3xyz+x^2y\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3x^2-2z\right)\right]\hat{i}+\left[\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(6xy+z^3\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3xyz+x^2y\right)\right]\hat{j}+\left[\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3x^2-2z\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(6xy+z^3\right)\right]\hat{k}\\=\left(3xz+x^2+2\right)\hat{i}+\left(3z^2-3yz-2xy\right)\hat{j}+(6x-6x)\hat{k}\\=\left(3xz+x^2+2\right)\hat{i}+\left(3z^2-3yz-2xy\right)\hat{j}+0\hat{k}\\\end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞, [math]\begin{array}{r}\vec{
abla}.(\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A})=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left\{\left(3 x z+x^{2}+2\right) \hat{i}\right. \left.+\left(3 z^{2}-3 y z-2 x y\right) \hat{j}+0 \hat{k}\right\}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{3.5cm}\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 x z+x^{2}+2\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3 z^{2}-3 y z-2 x y\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \times 0 \\=3 z+2 x-3 z-2 x \\=0\end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot(\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A})=0[/math]
‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot(\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A})[/math]
 ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§ [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá, 
[math]\nabla\times\vec A=(\partial_y A_z-\partial_z A_y)\hat i+(\partial_z A_x-\partial_x A_z)\hat j+(\partial_x A_y-\partial_y A_x)\hat k[/math], ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá
[math]\nabla\times\vec A=(3xz+x^2+2)\hat i+(3z^2-3yz-2xy)\hat j+0\hat k[/math]. ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡ßü ‚Äî ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™ [math](x,y,z)=(0,0,0)[/math]-‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ü‡¶ø [math]2[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\times\vec A=0[/math] ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡ßü‡•§

Question #19 (ID: 395685)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Barisal Cadet College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø [math]\vec{A}=\left(6 \mathrm{xy}+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-2 \mathrm{z}\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 \mathrm{xyz}+x^{2} y\right) \hat{k}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ò. (1, ‚àí 2, 1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{A}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\vec{A}=\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-2 z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x y z+x^{2} y\right) \hat{k}[/math]
‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤, [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}=\vec{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}[/math]
‚Äò‡¶ó' ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á, [math]\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A}=\left(3 x z+x^{2}+2\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 z^{2}-3 y z-2 x y\right) \hat{j}[/math]
 [math]\therefore(1,-2,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A} & =\left(3 \times 1 \times 1+1^{2}+1+2\right) \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\left\{3 \times 1^{2}-3 \times(-2) \times 1-2 \times 1 \times(-2)\right\} \hat{\mathrm{j}} \\& =5 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+13 \hat{\mathrm{j}} \\\vec{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} & 
eq 0\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡•§‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞, [math]\operatorname{div} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}=\vec{
abla} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{2.5cm}\begin{array}{l}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left\{\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}\right. \left.+\left(3 x^{2}-2 z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x y z+x^{2} y\right) \hat{k}\right\} \\=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 x^{2}-2 z\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 x y z+x^{2} y\right) \\=6 y+0+3 x y \\=6 y+3 x y\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore(1,-2,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{A}=6 \times(-2)+3 \times 1 \times(-2)[/math]
 [math]\hspace{4.7cm}=-12-6=-18[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶ò ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏: [math]\nabla\cdot\vec{A}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(6xy+z^3)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(3x^2-2z)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(3xyz+x^2y)=6y+0+3xy=y(6+3x)[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\cdot\vec{A}(1,-2,1)=-18[/math]. ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤: [math]\nabla\times\vec{A}=\Big(3xz+x^2+2,\;3z^2-3yz-2xy,\;0\Big)[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\nabla\times\vec{A}(1,-2,1)=(6,13,0)[/math]. ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ (rotational)‡•§

‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶§‡¶≤ ‡¶≠‡ßÇ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶°‡¶º‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÉ‡¶ï ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶£ 5 N‡•§

Options:
‡¶ó. ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ OC ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶§?

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]AO[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]BO[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÉ‡¶ï ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶£ [math]5 N[/math]
 ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç [math]OA[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]OB[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® [math]5 N.[/math]
 [math]OA[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]OB[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£, [math]\alpha=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{OC}[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® [math]R[/math]
 ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá,[math]\hspace{1.5 cm}\begin{aligned}\mathrm{R} & =\sqrt{5^{2}+5^{2}+2 \times 5 \times 5 \times \cos 60^{\circ}} \\ & =\sqrt{25+25+50 \times \dfrac{1}{2}}=8.66 \mathrm{~N} \end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶è‡¶¨, [math]OC[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® [math]8.66 ~N[/math]

‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ó ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá [math]5+5=[10\ \text{N}][/math]‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ (wing) ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá [math]5\ \text{N}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤ [math]10\ \text{N}[/math] ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º (‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶®‚Äì‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÇ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ)‡•§

Question #21 (ID: 395611)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Rajshahi University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
p ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{V}=(5 x+2 y) \vec{i}+(2 p y-z) \vec{j}+(x-2 z) \vec{k}[/math] ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßü‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\vec{v}=(5 x+2 y) \vec{i}+(2 p y-z) \vec{j}+(x-2 z) \vec{k}[/math]
 [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{V}=\frac{\partial(5 x+2 y)}{\partial x}+\frac{\partial(2 p y-z)}{\partial y}+\frac{\partial(x-2 x)}{\partial z}=0 \Rightarrow 5+2 p-2=0 \Rightarrow p=-\frac{3}{2}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßü‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\cdot\vec V=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(5x+2y)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(2py-z)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(x-2z)=5+2p-2=2p+3[/math].  
‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]2p+3=0[/math] ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá [math]p=-\tfrac{3}{2}[/math] ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Question #22 (ID: 395612)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Chittagong University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
a, b ‡¶ì c ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{V}=(x+y+a z) \hat{i}+(b x+3 y-z) \hat{j}+(3 x+c y+z) \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]
abla \times \vec{V}=0 \Rightarrow[/math]
 $\begin{vmatrix} \hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\ \frac{\partial}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\x+y+az & bx+3y-z & 3x+cy+z\end{vmatrix} = 0$[math]\Rightarrow \hat{i}(c+1)+\hat{j}(a-3)+\hat{k}(b-1)=0 \Rightarrow a=3, b=1, c=-1[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla\times\vec V=0[/math] ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á [math](\nabla\times\vec V)_x=c+1,\;(\nabla\times\vec V)_y=a-3,\;(\nabla\times\vec V)_z=b-1[/math], ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]a=3,\;b=1,\;c=-1[/math] ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

Question #23 (ID: 395613)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ [math]\vec{P}=\hat{i} t^{2}-\hat{j} t+\hat{k}(2 t+1)[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{Q}=\hat{i} 5 t+ \hat{j} t[/math] [math]-\hat{\mathrm{k}}^{3} t^{3}[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\frac{\mathrm{d}}{d t}(\vec{P} \cdot \vec{Q})[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\frac{d}{d t}(\vec{P} \times \vec{Q})[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(Answaer : [math]-8 t^{3}+12 t^{2}-2 t[/math]
 , ‡¶ì [math]\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left(4 \mathrm{t}^{3}-4 \mathrm{t}-1\right)+\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(5 \mathrm{t}^{4}+20 \mathrm{t}+5\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(3 \mathrm{t}^{2}+10 \mathrm{t}\right)[/math]
 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{r}\vec{A}=\hat{i t}^{2}-\hat{j} t+(2 t+1) \hat{k} \\\quad \vec{B}=5 \hat{i} t+\hat{j} t-\hat{k} t^{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{r}\therefore \frac{d}{d t}(\vec{A} \cdot \vec{B})=? \\\quad \frac{d}{d t}(\vec{A} \times \vec{B})=?\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{A} \cdot \vec{B} & =A_{x} B_{x}+A_{y} B_{y}+A_{z} B_{z} \\& =\left(t^{2}\right)(5 t)+(-t)(t)+(2 t+1)\left(-t^{3}\right) \\& =5 t^{3}-t^{2}-2 t^{4}-t^{3}=-2 t^{4}+4 t^{3}-t^{2}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}(\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}})=\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}\left(-2 \mathrm{t}^{4}+4 \mathrm{t}^{3}-\mathrm{t}^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=-2 \times 4 t^{3}+4 \times\left(3 t^{2}\right)-2 t=-8 t^{3}+12 t^{2}-2 t \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞,[math]\vec{A} \times \vec{B}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\t^{2} & -t & (2 t+1) \\5 t & t & -t^{3}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\hat{i}\left\{(-t)\left(-t^{3}\right)-(2 t+1) t\right\}-\hat{j}\left\{\left(t^{2}\right)\left(-t^{3}\right)\right.[/math]
 [math]-(2 \mathrm{t}+1)(5 \mathrm{t})\}+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left\{\left(\mathrm{t}^{2}\right)(\mathrm{t})-(-\mathrm{t})(5 \mathrm{t})\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\hat{i}\left(t^{4}-2 t^{2}-t\right)-\hat{j}\left(-t^{5}-10 t^{2}-5 t\right)+\hat{k}\left(t^{3}+5 t^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}(\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}})[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}\left\{\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left(\mathrm{t}^{4}-2 \mathrm{t}^{2}-\mathrm{t}\right)-\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(-\mathrm{t}^{5}-10 \mathrm{t}^{2}-5 \mathrm{t}\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(\mathrm{t}^{3}+5 \mathrm{t}^{2}\right)\right\} \\=\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left(4 \mathrm{t}^{3}-4 . t-1\right)-\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(-5 \mathrm{t}^{4}-20 \mathrm{t}-5\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(3 \mathrm{t}^{2}+10 \mathrm{t}\right) \\=\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left(4 \mathrm{t}^{3}-4 \mathrm{t}-1\right)+\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(5 \mathrm{t}^{4}+20 \mathrm{t}+5\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(3 \mathrm{t}^{2}+10 \mathrm{t}\right) \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø product rule ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\frac{d}{dt}(\vec P\cdot\vec Q)=\vec P'\cdot\vec Q+\vec P\cdot\vec Q'[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\frac{d}{dt}(\vec P\times\vec Q)=\vec P'\times\vec Q+\vec P\times\vec Q'[/math]. ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü [math]\vec P\cdot\vec Q=-6t^{4}+2t^{3}-t^{2}[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\frac{d}{dt}(\vec P\cdot\vec Q)=-24t^{3}+6t^{2}-2t[/math]. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\frac{d}{dt}(\vec P\times\vec Q)=(12t^{3}-4t-1)\,\hat{i}+(15t^{4}+20t+5)\,\hat{j}+(3t^{2}+10t)\,\hat{k}[/math], ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ product rule ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

Question #24 (ID: 395614)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\phi(x, y, z)=2 x z^{4}-x^{2} y[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math](2,-2,-1)[/math] ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla} \phi[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\m id \vec{
abla}_{\phi}\mid[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã ‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(Answer : [math]10 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-4 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-16 \hat{\mathrm{k}}[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]2 \sqrt{93}[/math]
 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l}\phi(x, y, z)=2 x z^{4}-x^{2} y \\\vec{
abla}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,[math]\begin{aligned}\phi & =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \\& \left(2 x z^{4}-x^{2} y\right) \\& =\left(2 z^{4}-2 x y\right) \hat{i}-x^{2} \hat{j}+8 x z^{3} \hat{k}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math](2,-2,-1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla}_{\phi}=\left\{2(-1)^{4}-2(2)(-2)\right\} \hat{i}-(2)^{2} \hat{j}[/math]
 [math]+\left\{8(2)(1)^{3}\right\} \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]=(2+8) \hat{\mathrm{i}}-4 \hat{j}-16 \hat{k}=10 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-4 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-16 \hat{\mathrm{k}}(\text { Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\left|\vec{
abla}_{\phi}\right| & =\sqrt{10^{2}+(-4)^{2}+(-16)^{2}} \\& =2 \sqrt{93} \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\phi=(\phi_x,\phi_y,\phi_z)=(2z^4-2xy,\,-x^2,\;8xz^3)[/math]. (2,-2,-1) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla\phi(2,-2,-1)=(10,-4,-16)[/math]. ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé [math]|\nabla\phi|=\sqrt{10^2+(-4)^2+(-16)^2}=\sqrt{372}=2\sqrt{93}[/math].

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
[math]\vec{
abla} \cdot\left(2 x^{2} z \hat{i}-x y^{2} z \hat{j}+3 y z^{2} \hat{k}\righ t)[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(Answer : [math]4 x z-2 x y z+6 y z[/math]
)[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø, [math]\vec{
abla}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® , [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot\left(2 x^{2} z \hat{i}-x y^{2} z \hat{j}+3 y z^{2} \hat{k}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z^{2}} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left(2 x^{2} z \hat{i}-x y^{2} z \hat{j}+3 y z^{2} \hat{k}\right) \\=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(2 x^{2} z\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(-x y^{2} z\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(3 y z^{2}\right) \\=4 x z-2 x y z+6 y z \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó; ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\cdot F=\frac{\partial(2x^2 z)}{\partial x}+\frac{\partial(-x y^2 z)}{\partial y}+\frac{\partial(3 y z^2)}{\partial z}[/math]. ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\frac{\partial(2x^2 z)}{\partial x}=4xz,\;\frac{\partial(-x y^2 z)}{\partial y}=-2xyz,\;\frac{\partial(3 y z^2)}{\partial z}=6yz[/math],‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá [math]4xz-2xyz+6yz[/math]‡•§

Question #26 (ID: 395616)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
[math]\phi=2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{
abla} \phi[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã ‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(Answer : [math]12 x y^{2} z^{4}+4 x^{3} z^{4}+24 x^{3} y^{2} z^{2}[/math]
 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\phi=2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}[/math]
 [math]\vec{
abla}_{\phi}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right)\left(2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}\right) \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}\right) \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}\right) \hat{k} \\=6 x^{2} y^{2} z^{4} \hat{i}+4 x^{3} y z^{4} \hat{j}+8 x^{3} y^{2} z^{3} \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,[math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{
abla} \phi=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left(6 x^{2} y^{2} z^{4} \hat{i}+4 x^{3} y z^{4} \hat{j}\right.[/math]
 [math]\left.+8 x^{3} y^{2} z^{3} \hat{k}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(6 x^{2} y^{2} z^{4}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(4 x^{3} y z^{4}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(8 x^{3} y^{2} z^{3}\right) \\=12 x y^{2} z^{4}+4 x^{3} z^{4}+24 x^{3} y^{2} z^{2} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: [math]‚àá\cdot‚àáœÜ=‚àá^2œÜ=\frac{‚àÇ^2œÜ}{‚àÇx^2}+\frac{‚àÇ^2œÜ}{‚àÇy^2}+\frac{‚àÇ^2œÜ}{‚àÇz^2}[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á œÜ-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ü‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]œÜ=2x^3y^2z^4[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\frac{‚àÇ^2œÜ}{‚àÇx^2}=12x y^2 z^4,\quad \frac{‚àÇ^2œÜ}{‚àÇy^2}=4x^3 z^4,\quad \frac{‚àÇ^2œÜ}{‚àÇz^2}=24x^3 y^2 z^2[/math], ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá [math]‚àá^2œÜ=12x y^2 z^4+4x^3 z^4+24x^3 y^2 z^2[/math]‡•§

Question #27 (ID: 395617)

Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
[math]\vec{A}=3 x y z^{2} \hat{\mathbf{i}}+2 x y^{3} \hat{j}-x^{2} y z \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\ phi 
eq 3 x^{2}-y z[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math](1,-1,1)[/math] ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞ [math]\text { (a) } \vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{A}(\text { (b) } \vec{A} \cdot \vec{
abla} \phi(c) \vec{
abla} \cdot(\phi \vec{A}) \text { (d) } \vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{
abla} \phi[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(Answer : (a) 4 (b) [math]-15[/math]
 (c) 1 (d) 6 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l}\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}=3 x y z^{2} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 x y^{3} \hat{\mathrm{j}}-\mathrm{x}^{2} y z \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\\phi=3 \mathrm{x}^{2}-\mathrm{yz} \\\vec{
abla}=\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}} \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{\mathrm{k}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{i}} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}} \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{k}} \hat{\mathrm{k}}\right)[/math]
 [math]\left(3 x y z^{2} \hat{i}+2 x y^{3} \hat{j}-\right.[/math]
 [math]\left.x^{2} y z \hat{k}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x} 3 x y z^{2}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} 2 x y^{3}-\frac{\partial}{\partial z} x^{2} y z \\=3 y z^{2}+6 x y^{2}-x^{2} y\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, [math](1,-1,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\begin{aligned}\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{A} & =3(-1)(1)^{2}+6 \cdot 1(-1)^{2}-(1)^{2}(-1) \\& =-3+6+1=4 \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]
(b) [math]\begin{aligned}\vec{
abla}_{\phi} & =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left(3 x^{2}-y z\right) \\& =6 x \hat{i}-z \hat{j}-y \hat{k}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math](1,-1,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla}_{\phi}=6 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-\hat{\mathrm{j}}+\hat{k}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{A} \cdot \vec{
abla} \phi & =\left(3 x y z^{2} \hat{i}+2 x y^{3} \hat{j}-x^{2} y z \hat{k}\right) \cdot(6 \hat{i}-\hat{j}+\hat{k}) \\& =18 x y z^{2}-2 x y^{3}-x^{2} y z\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math](1,-1,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{A} \cdot \vec{
abla}_{\phi}=-18+2+1 \doteq-15 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
(c),[math]\begin{aligned}\phi \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} & =\left(3 x^{2}-y z\right)\left(3 x y z^{2} \hat{i}+2 x y^{3} \hat{j}-x^{2} y z \hat{k}\right) \\& =\left(9 x^{3} y z^{2}-3 x y^{2} z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(6 x^{3} y^{3}-2 x y^{4} z\right) \hat{j}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]+\left(-3 x^{4} y z+x^{2} y^{2} z^{2}\right) \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot(\phi \vec{A})=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(9 x^{3} y z^{2}-3 x y^{2} z^{3}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(6 x^{3} y^{3}-2 x y^{4} z\right)[/math]
 [math]+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(-3 x^{4} y z+x^{2} y^{2} z^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=27 x^{2} y z^{2}-3 y^{2} z^{3}+18 x^{3} y^{2}-8 x y^{3} z-3 x^{4} y+2 x^{2} y^{2} z[/math]
 [math](1,-1,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ,[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{
abla} \cdot(\phi \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}) & =-27-3+18+8+3+2 \\& =-30+31=1 \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]
(d),[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{
abla}_{\phi} & =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left(3 x^{2}-y z\right) \\& =6 x \hat{i}-z \hat{j}-y \hat{k}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{
abla} \phi & =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot(6 x \hat{i}-z \hat{j}-y \hat{k}) \\& =6-0+0=6 \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:

‡¶ï [math]\nabla\cdot\vec{A}=\partial_x(3xyz^2)+\partial_y(2xy^3)+\partial_z(-x^2yz)=3yz^2+6xy^2-x^2y[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\cdot\vec{A}(1,-1,1)=-3+6+1=4[/math].

‡¶ñ [math]\nabla\phi=(6x,-z,-y)\Rightarrow\nabla\phi(1,-1,1)=(6,-1,1)[/math], ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{A}(1,-1,1)=(-3,-2,1)[/math], ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç [math]\vec{A}\cdot\nabla\phi=-3\cdot6+(-2)(-1)+1\cdot1=-15[/math]‡•§

‡¶ó ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø [math]\nabla\cdot(\phi\vec{A})=\vec{A}\cdot\nabla\phi+\phi\,\nabla\cdot\vec{A}[/math]; ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\vec{A}\cdot\nabla\phi=-15,\ \phi(1,-1,1)=3-(-1)=4,\ \nabla\cdot\vec{A}=4[/math], ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla\cdot(\phi\vec{A})=-15+4\cdot4=1[/math]‡•§

‡¶ò [math]\nabla\cdot\nabla\phi=\nabla^2\phi=\partial_{xx}\phi+\partial_{yy}\phi+\partial_{zz}\phi=6+0+0=6[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® = [math]6[/math]‡•§

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßá , [math]\vec{A}=3 y^{4} z^{2} \hat{i}+4 x^{3} z^{2} \hat{j}-3 x^{2} y^{2} \hat{k }[/math] ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßü‡ßá‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Solution :[math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}=3 \mathrm{y}^{4} z^{2} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+4 x^{3} z^{2} \hat{\mathrm{j}}-3 x^{2} y^{2} \hat{\mathrm{k}}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{A}=0[/math]
 ‡¶π‡ßü ‡•§[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{
abla} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} & =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z^{2}} \hat{\mathrm{k}}\right) \cdot\left(3 y^{4} z^{2} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+4 x^{3} z^{3} \hat{\mathrm{j}}-3 x^{2} y^{2} \hat{\mathrm{k}}\right) \\& =\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 y^{4} z^{2}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(4 x^{3} z^{3}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(-3 x^{2} y^{2}\right) \\& =0+0-0=0\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ( Showed)

Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ï (divergence) ‡¶π‡¶≤ [math]\nabla\cdot\vec{A}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(3y^4z^2)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(4x^3z^2)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(-3x^2y^2)=0+0+0=0[/math]. ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec{A}[/math] ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßü‡ßá‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ (divergence ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø)‡•§

Question #29 (ID: 395619)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\vec{A}=2 x^{2} \hat{i}-x y \hat{j}+3 x z^{3} \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\phi=x^{2} y z[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math](1,1,1)[/math] ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞ [math]\text { (a) } \vec{
abla} \times \vec{A} \text { (b) } \vec{
abla} \times(\phi \vec{A}) \text { (c) } \vec{
abla} \times(\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A})[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(Answer : (a) [math]\hat{j}-\hat{k}[/math]
 (b) [math]4 \hat{i}-3 \hat{j}-5 \hat{k}[/math]
 (c) 0 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\vec{A}=2 x z^{2} \hat{i}-x y \hat{j}+[/math]
 [math]3 x z^{3} \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\phi=x^{2} y z[/math]
(a),[math]\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\\frac{\partial}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\2 x z^{2} & -x y & 3 x z^{3}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3 x z^{3}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(-x y)\right\} \hat{i}-\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 x z^{3}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2 x z^{2}\right)\right\} \hat{j}[/math]
 [math]+\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(-x y)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(2 x z^{2}\right)\right\} \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=(0-0) \hat{\mathbf{i}}-\left(3 z^{3}-4 x z\right) \hat{j}+(-y) \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\=\left(4 x z-3 z^{3}\right) \hat{j}-y \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
 [math](1,1,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A}=\hat{j}-\hat{k} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
(b),[math]\begin{aligned}\phi \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} & =\left(x^{2} y \mathrm{z}\right)\left(2 x z^{2} \hat{i}-x y \hat{j}+3 x z^{3} \hat{k}\right) \\& =2 x^{3} y z^{3} \hat{i}-x^{3} y^{2} z \hat{j}+3 x^{3} y z^{4} \hat{k}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\vec{
abla} \times \phi \vec{A} & =\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{\mathrm{i}} & \hat{\mathrm{j}} & \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\2 \mathrm{x}^{3} y z^{3} & -\mathrm{x}^{3} \mathrm{y}^{2} z & 3 \mathrm{x}^{3} y \mathrm{z}^{4}\end{array}\right| \\& =\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}}\left(3 \mathrm{x}^{3} y z^{4}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(\mathrm{x}^{3} y^{2} z\right)\right\} \hat{\mathrm{i}}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}-\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 x^{3} y z^{4}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2 x^{3} y z^{3}\right)\right\} \hat{j} \\+\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(-x^{3} y^{2} z\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(2 x^{3} y z^{3}\right)\right\} \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\left(3 x^{3} z^{4}+x^{3} y^{2}\right) \hat{i}-\left(9 x^{2} y z^{4}-6 x^{3} y z^{2}\right) \hat{j}[/math]
 [math]+\left(-3 x^{2} y^{2} z-2 x^{3} z^{3}\right) \hat{k}[/math]
 [math](1,1,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla} \times \phi \vec{A}=(3+1) \hat{i}-(9-6) \hat{j}+(-5) \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]=4 \hat{i}-3 \hat{j}-5 \hat{k} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
(c), [math]\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A}=\hat{j}-\hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\vec{
abla} \times(\vec{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}})=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{\mathrm{i}} & \hat{\mathrm{j}} & \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}} & \frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\0 & 1 & -1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(-1)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(1)\right\} \hat{i}-\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(-1)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(0)\right\} \hat{j}[/math]
 [math]+\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}}(0)-\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}}(-1)\right\} \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]=0 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:

‡¶ï [math]\vec{\nabla}\times\vec{A}=\begin{vmatrix}\hat{i}&\hat{j}&\hat{k}\\
\partial_x&\partial_y&\partial_z\\
2x^2&-xy&3xz^3\end{vmatrix}=0\hat{i}-3z^{3}\hat{j}-y\hat{k}[/math], ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç [math](1,1,1)[/math]-‡¶è [math]-3\hat{j}-\hat{k}[/math]‡•§

‡¶ñ ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá-‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÇ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ [math]\vec{\nabla}\times(\phi\vec{A})=\vec{\nabla}\phi\times\vec{A}+\phi(\vec{\nabla}\times\vec{A})[/math] ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{\nabla}\phi=(2xy z,x^2 z,x^2 y)=(2,1,1)[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\vec{A}=(2,-1,3)[/math] (‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{\nabla}\times\vec{A}=(0,-3,-1)[/math], ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü [math](4,-4,-4)+(0,-3,-1)=(4,-7,-5)=4\hat{i}-7\hat{j}-5\hat{k}[/math]‡•§

‡¶ó ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶Ø‡¶º [math]\vec{\nabla}\times(\vec{\nabla}\times\vec{A})=\vec{\nabla}(\vec{\nabla}\cdot\vec{A})-\nabla^{2}\vec{A}[/math] ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{\nabla}\cdot\vec{A}=3x+9xz^2[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec{\nabla}(\vec{\nabla}\cdot\vec{A})=(3+9z^2,0,18xz)[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\nabla^{2}\vec{A}=(4,0,18xz)[/math], ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá (1,1,1) ‡¶è ‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤ [math](8,0,0)=8\hat{i}[/math]‡•§
