Question #68 (ID: 395661)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ [math]\vec{P}=\hat{i} t^{2}-\hat{j} t+\hat{k}(2 t+1)[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{Q}=\hat{i} 5 t+ \hat{j} t[/math] [math]-\hat{\mathrm{k}}^{}\ t^{3}[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\frac{\mathrm{d}}{d t}(\vec{P} \cdot \vec{Q})[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\frac{d}{d t}(\vec{P} \times \vec{Q})[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(Answaer : [math]-8 t^{3}+12 t^{2}-2 t[/math]
 , ‡¶ì [math]\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left(4 \mathrm{t}^{3}-4 \mathrm{t}-1\right)+\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(5 \mathrm{t}^{4}+20 \mathrm{t}+5\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(3 \mathrm{t}^{2}+10 \mathrm{t}\right)[/math]
 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{r}\vec{A}=\hat{i t}^{2}-\hat{j} t+(2 t+1) \hat{k} \\\quad \vec{B}=5 \hat{i} t+\hat{j} t-\hat{k} t^{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{r}\therefore \frac{d}{d t}(\vec{A} \cdot \vec{B})=? \\\quad \frac{d}{d t}(\vec{A} \times \vec{B})=?\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{A} \cdot \vec{B} & =A_{x} B_{x}+A_{y} B_{y}+A_{z} B_{z} \\& =\left(t^{2}\right)(5 t)+(-t)(t)+(2 t+1)\left(-t^{3}\right) \\& =5 t^{3}-t^{2}-2 t^{4}-t^{3}=-2 t^{4}+4 t^{3}-t^{2}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}(\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}})=\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}\left(-2 \mathrm{t}^{4}+4 \mathrm{t}^{3}-\mathrm{t}^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=-2 \times 4 t^{3}+4 \times\left(3 t^{2}\right)-2 t=-8 t^{3}+12 t^{2}-2 t \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞,[math]\vec{A} \times \vec{B}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\t^{2} & -t & (2 t+1) \\5 t & t & -t^{3}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\hat{i}\left\{(-t)\left(-t^{3}\right)-(2 t+1) t\right\}-\hat{j}\left\{\left(t^{2}\right)\left(-t^{3}\right)\right.[/math]
 [math]-(2 \mathrm{t}+1)(5 \mathrm{t})\}+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left\{\left(\mathrm{t}^{2}\right)(\mathrm{t})-(-\mathrm{t})(5 \mathrm{t})\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\hat{i}\left(t^{4}-2 t^{2}-t\right)-\hat{j}\left(-t^{5}-10 t^{2}-5 t\right)+\hat{k}\left(t^{3}+5 t^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}(\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}})[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}\left\{\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left(\mathrm{t}^{4}-2 \mathrm{t}^{2}-\mathrm{t}\right)-\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(-\mathrm{t}^{5}-10 \mathrm{t}^{2}-5 \mathrm{t}\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(\mathrm{t}^{3}+5 \mathrm{t}^{2}\right)\right\} \\=\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left(4 \mathrm{t}^{3}-4 . t-1\right)-\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(-5 \mathrm{t}^{4}-20 \mathrm{t}-5\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(3 \mathrm{t}^{2}+10 \mathrm{t}\right) \\=\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left(4 \mathrm{t}^{3}-4 \mathrm{t}-1\right)+\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(5 \mathrm{t}^{4}+20 \mathrm{t}+5\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(3 \mathrm{t}^{2}+10 \mathrm{t}\right) \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®: ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø [math]\frac{d}{dt}(\vec P\cdot\vec Q)=\vec P'\cdot\vec Q+\vec P\cdot\vec Q'[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\frac{d}{dt}(\vec P\times\vec Q)=\vec P'\times\vec Q+\vec P\times\vec Q'[/math], ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\vec P'=(2t,-1,2)[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec Q'=(5,1,-3t^2)[/math]. ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á:

‡¶ï [math]\frac{d}{dt}(\vec P\cdot\vec Q)=-8t^3+12t^2-2t[/math].

‡¶ñ [math]\frac{d}{dt}(\vec P\times\vec Q)=\hat{i}(4t^3-4t-1)+\hat{j}(5t^4+20t+5)+\hat{k}(3t^2+10t)[/math].

Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßá, [math]\operatorname{div} \vec{r}=3[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Solution :‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞, [math]\vec{r}=x \hat{i}+y \hat{j}+z \hat{k}[/math]
‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶∞, [math]\vec{
abla}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right)[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, [math]\operatorname{div} \vec{\mathrm{r}}=\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{\mathrm{r}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot(x \hat{i}+y \hat{j}+z \hat{k}) \\=\frac{\partial x}{\partial x}+\frac{\partial y}{\partial y}+\frac{\partial z}{\partial z}=1+1+1=3\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \operatorname{div} \vec{r}=3 \quad \text { [Showed] }[/math]

Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ [math]\vec{r}=\hat{i} \cos \omega t+\hat{j} \sin \omega t[/math] (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]{\omega}[/math]‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ï)‡•§ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßá, [math]\vec{r}[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\vec{v}[/math] ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{r}\times[/math] [math]\vec{v}[/math] ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Solution :‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá,[math]\vec{r}=\hat{i} \cos \omega t+\hat{j} \sin \omega t[/math]
‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ó [math]\vec{v}=?[/math]
‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶£ [math]\vec{a}=?[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{v} & =\frac{d \vec{r}}{d t} \\& =\frac{d}{d t}(\hat{i} \cos \omega t+\hat{j} \sin \omega t)\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{d}{d t}(\hat{i} \cos \omega t)+\frac{d}{d t}(\hat{j} \sin \omega t) \\=-\omega \hat{i} \sin \omega t+\omega \hat{j} \cos \omega t \\=\omega(-\hat{i} \sin \omega t+\hat{j} \cos \omega t) \text { (Ans. ) }\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{a} & =\frac{d \vec{v}}{d t} \\& =\frac{d}{d t}\{\omega(-\hat{i} \sin \omega t+\hat{j} \cos \omega t)\} \\& =\omega(-\omega \hat{i} \cos \omega t-\omega \hat{j} \sin \omega t) \\& =-\omega^{2}(\hat{i} \cos \omega t+\hat{j} \sin \omega t)=-\omega^{2} \vec{r} \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ,[math]\vec{\mathrm{r}} \times \vec{\mathrm{v}}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\\cos \omega t & \sin \omega t & 0 \\-\omega \sin \omega t & \omega \cos \omega t & 0\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\hat{k}\left(\omega \cos ^{2} \omega t+\omega \sin ^{2} \omega t\right)[/math]
 [math]=\hat{\mathrm{k}} \omega=[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ (‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§)

Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø: [math]\vec{v}=\frac{d\vec{r}}{dt}=-\omega\hat{i}\sin\omega t+\omega\hat{j}\cos\omega t[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec{r}\cdot\vec{v}=\cos\omega t(-\omega\sin\omega t)+\sin\omega t(\omega\cos\omega t)=0[/math], ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{r}[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\vec{v}[/math] ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá: [math]\vec{r}\times\vec{v}=\hat{k}\,\omega(\cos^2\omega t+\sin^2\omega t)=\omega\hat{k}[/math], ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡•§

Question #75 (ID: 395670)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßá, [math]\vec{
abla} \times(\vec{
abla} \varphi)=0[/math] ‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ, [math]\text { Curl} \v arphi=0[/math] ‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Solution :[math]\text { (ii) } \vec{
abla} \times \vec{
abla} \varphi[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\vec{
abla} \times\left(\hat{i} \frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}}+\hat{\mathrm{j}} \cdot \frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}}+\hat{\mathrm{k}} \frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{z}}\right) \varphi \\=\vec{
abla} \times\left(\hat{i} \frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{x}}+\hat{\mathrm{j}} \frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{y}}+\hat{\mathrm{k}} \frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{z}}\right) \text {. } \\=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\\frac{\partial}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial z}\end{array}\right| \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left[\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}}\left(\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{z}}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{z}}\left(\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{y}}\right)\right]+\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left[\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{z}}\left(\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{x}}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}}\left(\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{z}}\right)\right] \\+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left[\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}}\left(\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{y}}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}}\left(\frac{\partial \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{x}}\right)\right] \\=\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left(\frac{\partial^{2} \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{y} \partial \mathrm{z}}-\frac{\partial^{2} \varphi}{\partial z \partial \mathrm{y}}\right)+\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(\frac{\partial^{2} \varphi}{\partial z \partial \mathrm{x}}-\frac{\partial^{2} \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{x} \partial \mathrm{z}}\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\left(\frac{\partial^{2} \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{x} \partial \mathrm{y}}-\frac{\partial^{2} \varphi}{\partial \mathrm{x} \partial \mathrm{y}}\right) \\=\hat{\mathrm{i}} \cdot 0+\hat{\mathrm{j}} \cdot 0+\hat{\mathrm{k}} \cdot 0=0\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: [math]\nabla\times(\nabla\varphi)=\Big(\frac{\partial^2\varphi}{\partial y\partial z}-\frac{\partial^2\varphi}{\partial z\partial y},\;\frac{\partial^2\varphi}{\partial z\partial x}-\frac{\partial^2\varphi}{\partial x\partial z},\;\frac{\partial^2\varphi}{\partial x\partial y}-\frac{\partial^2\varphi}{\partial y\partial x}\Big)[/math]. ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶á ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßÉ‡¶£‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla\times(\nabla\varphi)=0[/math].

Question #76 (ID: 395671)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\phi=2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{
abla} \phi[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(Answer : [math]12 x y^{2} z^{4}+4 x^{3} z^{4}+24 x^{3} y^{2} z^{2}[/math]
 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\phi=2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}[/math]
 [math]\vec{
abla}_{\phi}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right)\left(2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}\right) \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}\right) \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2 x^{3} y^{2} z^{4}\right) \hat{k} \\=6 x^{2} y^{2} z^{4} \hat{i}+4 x^{3} y z^{4} \hat{j}+8 x^{3} y^{2} z^{3} \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,[math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{
abla} \phi=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left(6 x^{2} y^{2} z^{4} \hat{i}+4 x^{3} y z^{4} \hat{j}\right.[/math]
 [math]\left.+8 x^{3} y^{2} z^{3} \hat{k}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(6 x^{2} y^{2} z^{4}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(4 x^{3} y z^{4}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(8 x^{3} y^{2} z^{3}\right) \\=12 x y^{2} z^{4}+4 x^{3} z^{4}+24 x^{3} y^{2} z^{2} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\nabla\cdot\nabla\phi=\nabla^{2}\phi[/math] (Laplacian) ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡•§ ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º [math]\frac{\partial\phi}{\partial x}=6x^{2}y^{2}z^{4},\ \frac{\partial^{2}\phi}{\partial x^{2}}=12xy^{2}z^{4},\ \frac{\partial^{2}\phi}{\partial y^{2}}=4x^{3}z^{4},\ \frac{\partial^{2}\phi}{\partial z^{2}}=24x^{3}y^{2}z^{2}[/math]. ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\nabla^{2}\phi=12xy^{2}z^{4}+4x^{3}z^{4}+24x^{3}y^{2}z^{2}[/math], ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§

Question:
[math]\phi(x, y, z)=2 x z^{4}-x^{2} y[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math](2,-2,-1)[/math] ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla} \phi[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\m id \vec{
abla}_{\phi}\mid[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã ‡•§

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(Answer : [math]10 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-4 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-16 \hat{\mathrm{k}}[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]2 \sqrt{93}[/math]
 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l}\phi(x, y, z)=2 x z^{4}-x^{2} y \\\vec{
abla}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,[math]\begin{aligned}\phi & =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \\& \left(2 x z^{4}-x^{2} y\right) \\& =\left(2 z^{4}-2 x y\right) \hat{i}-x^{2} \hat{j}+8 x z^{3} \hat{k}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math](2,-2,-1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla}_{\phi}=\left\{2(-1)^{4}-2(2)(-2)\right\} \hat{i}-(2)^{2} \hat{j}[/math]
 [math]+\left\{8(2)(1)^{3}\right\} \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]=(2+8) \hat{\mathrm{i}}-4 \hat{j}-16 \hat{k}=10 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-4 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-16 \hat{\mathrm{k}}(\text { Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\left|\vec{
abla}_{\phi}\right| & =\sqrt{10^{2}+(-4)^{2}+(-16)^{2}} \\& =2 \sqrt{93} \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®: ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá [math]\phi_x=2z^4-2xy,\;\phi_y=-x^2,\;\phi_z=8xz^3[/math], ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç [math]\vec{\nabla}\phi=(2z^4-2xy,\,-x^2,\,8xz^3)[/math]‡•§ ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{\nabla}\phi(2,-2,-1)=(10,-4,-16)[/math] ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá [math]|\vec{\nabla}\phi|=\sqrt{10^2+(-4)^2+(-16)^2}=\;2\sqrt{93}[/math]‡•§

Question:

eq 3 x^{2}-y z[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math](1,-1,1)[/math] ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞ [math]\text { (a) } \vec{

 [math]\vec{

 [math]\left.x^{2} y z \hat{k}\right)[/math]

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, [math](1,-1,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\begin{aligned}\vec{

 [math](1,-1,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{

 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{A} \cdot \vec{

 [math]+\left(-3 x^{4} y z+x^{2} y^{2} z^{2}\right) \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot(\phi \vec{A})=\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(9 x^{3} y z^{2}-3 x y^{2} z^{3}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(6 x^{3} y^{3}-2 x y^{4} z\right)[/math]

 [math]=27 x^{2} y z^{2}-3 y^{2} z^{3}+18 x^{3} y^{2}-8 x y^{3} z-3 x^{4} y+2 x^{2} y^{2} z[/math]
 [math](1,-1,1)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ,[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{

(d),[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{

 [math]\begin{aligned}\vec{

Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:

‡¶ï [math]\nabla\cdot\vec{A}=\partial_x(3xyz^2)+\partial_y(2xy^3)+\partial_z(-x^2yz)=3yz^2+6xy^2-x^2y[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math](1,-1,1)[/math]-‡¶è [math] -3+6+1=4[/math]‡•§ 

‡¶ñ Î®ºÏ†Ä [math]\nabla\phi=(6x)\hat{i}-z\hat{j}-y\hat{k}[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec{A}\cdot\nabla\phi=18x^2yz^2-2xy^3z+x^2y^2z[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math](1,-1,1)[/math]-‡¶è ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® = [math]-18+2+1=-15[/math]‡•§ 

‡¶ó [math]\nabla\cdot(\phi\vec{A})=\vec{A}\cdot\nabla\phi+\phi(\nabla\cdot\vec{A})[/math]; ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\phi(1,-1,1)=3(1)^2-(-1)(1)=4[/math], ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá [math]-15+4\cdot4=1[/math]‡•§ 

‡¶ò [math]\nabla\cdot\nabla\phi=\nabla^2\phi=\partial_{xx}\phi+\partial_{yy}\phi+\partial_{zz}\phi[/math]; [math]\phi=3x^2-yz[/math] ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá [math]\nabla^2\phi=6[/math] (‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á)‡•§

Question:
a ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ A ‡¶ì B ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\vec{A}=5 \hat{i}+2 \ hat{j}-3 \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{\mathrm{B}}=15 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+a \hat{\mathrm{j}}-9 \hat{k}[/math]

( Answer : [math]-8 t^{3}+12 t^{2}-2 t[/math]

Solution :‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l}\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}=5 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-3 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\\overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}}=15 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\hat{\mathrm{a}}-9 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\\mathrm{a}=?\end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\vec{A} \times \vec{B}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{\mathrm{i}} & \hat{\mathrm{j}} & \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\5 & 2 & -3 \\15 & \mathrm{a} & -9\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\hat{i}(-18+3 a)-\hat{j}(-45+45)+\hat{k}(5 a-30) \\=(3 a-18) \hat{i}+(5 a-30) \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, [math]\vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]\vec{B}[/math]
 ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø [math]|\vec{A} \times \vec{B}|=0[/math]
 ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§[math]\begin{aligned}\therefore & \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}(\vec{\mathrm{A}} \cdot \vec{\mathrm{B}})=? \\& \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}(\vec{A} \times \vec{B})=?\end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ,[math]\begin{aligned}\vec{\mathrm{A}} \cdot \vec{\mathrm{B}} & =\mathrm{A}_{x} \mathrm{~B}_{x}+\mathrm{A}_{y} \mathrm{~B}_{y}+\mathrm{A}_{z} \mathrm{~B}_{z} \\& =\left(\mathrm{t}^{2}\right)(5 \mathrm{t})+(-\mathrm{t})(\mathrm{t})+(2 \mathrm{t}+1)\left(-\mathrm{t}^{3}\right) \\& =5 \mathrm{t}^{3}-\mathrm{t}^{2}-2 \mathrm{t}^{4}-\mathrm{t}^{3}=-2 \mathrm{t}^{4}+4 \mathrm{t}^{3}-\mathrm{t}^{2}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}(\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}}) & =\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dt}}\left(-2 \mathrm{t}^{4}+4 \mathrm{t}^{3}-\mathrm{t}^{2}\right) \\& =-2 \times 4 t^{3}+4 \times\left(3 t^{2}\right)-2 t=-8 t^{3}+12 t^{2}-2 t \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞,[math]\vec{A} \times \vec{B}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\t^{2} & -t & (2 t+1) \\5 t & t & -t^{3}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\hat{i}\left\{(-t)\left(-t^{3}\right)-(2 t+1) t\right\}-\hat{j}\left\{\left(t^{2}\right)\left(-t^{3}\right)\right. \\\quad-(2 t+1)(5 t)\}+\hat{k}\left\{\left(t^{2}\right)(t)-(-t)(5 t)\right\} \\=\hat{i}\left(t^{4}-2 t^{2}-t\right)-\hat{j}\left(-t^{5}-10 t^{2}-5 t\right)+\hat{k}\left(t^{3}+5 t^{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \frac{d}{d t} & (\vec{A} \times \vec{B}) \\& =\frac{d}{d t}\left\{\hat{i}\left(t^{4}-2 t^{2}-t\right)-\hat{j}\left(-t^{5}-10 t^{2}-5 t\right)+\hat{k}\left(t^{3}+5 t^{2}\right)\right\} \\& =\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left(4 t^{3}-4 \cdot t-1\right)-\hat{j}\left(-5 t^{4}-20 t-5\right)+\hat{k}\left(3 t^{2}+10 t\right) \\& =\hat{i}\left(4 t^{3}-4 t-1\right)+\hat{j}\left(5 t^{4}+20 t+5\right)+\hat{k}\left(3 t^{2}+10 \mathrm{t}\right)(A n s .)\end{aligned}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ï ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\vec{A}=5\hat{i}+2\hat{j}-3\hat{k}[/math], [math]\vec{B}=15\hat{i}+a\hat{j}-9\hat{k}[/math]; ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]15=5k\Rightarrow k=3[/math]. ‡¶ó‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡ßá [math]a=2k=6[/math], ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]-9=-3k[/math] ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á [math]k=3[/math] ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá [math]a=6[/math]‡•§

Question #80 (ID: 395675)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® [math]x=\left(3.0 \mathrm{~ms}^{-2}\right) t+\left(2.0 \mathrm{~ms}^{-1}\right) t[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]y=\left(2 m^{-2}\right) t^{2}+\left(4 \mathrm{~ms}^{-1}\right) t[/math] ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

(i) ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ó ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶§ ?

(ii) ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ì ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ?

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
( Answer : (i) [math]6 \hat{i}+4 \hat{j}[/math]
 (ii) [math]7.2 \mathrm{~ms}^{-2}[/math]
 , [math]33.7^{\circ}[/math]
 )[math]\\[/math]
Solution :‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá,[math]x=\left(3.0 \mathrm{~ms}^{-2}\right) t^{2}+\left(2.0 \mathrm{~ms}^{-1}\right)[/math]
 t‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]y=\left(2{m s^{-2}}^{-2}\right) t^{2}+\left(4 \mathrm{~ms}^{-1}\right) t[/math]
(i) [math]\overrightarrow{v_{x}}=\frac{d x}{d t}=(6 t+2) \mathrm{ms}^{-1}[/math]
 [math]\vec{v}_{y}=\frac{d y}{d t}=(4 t+4) \mathrm{ms}^{-1}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \vec{v}=\overrightarrow{v_{x}}+\overrightarrow{v_{y}}=(6 t+2) \hat{i}+(4 t+4) \hat{j}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\overrightarrow{a_{x}}=\frac{d v_{x}}{d t}=6 \mathrm{~ms}^{-2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\quad\overrightarrow{a_y}&=\frac{dv_{\dot{y}}}{dt}=4\cdot\mathrm{ms}^{-2}\\\therefore\overrightarrow{a^{ }}=&\overrightarrow{a_x}+\overrightarrow{a_y}=6\hat{i}+4\hat{j}\end{aligned}[/math]
(ii) ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® [math]=|\vec{a}|=a=\sqrt{\left.(6)^{2}+(4)^{2}\right)}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\sqrt{36+16} \\=\sqrt{52}=7.2 \mathrm{~ms}^{-2} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞, [math]\tan \theta=\frac{a_{y}}{a_{x}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]\tan \theta=\frac{4}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\tan ^{-1}\left(\frac{4}{6}\right)=33.7^{\circ} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá [math]x=(3.0\ \mathrm{m\,s^{-2}})t^{2}+(2.0\ \mathrm{m\,s^{-1}})t[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]y=(2.0\ \mathrm{m\,s^{-2}})t^{2}+(4.0\ \mathrm{m\,s^{-1}})t[/math], ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶®  
[math]\vec v=\frac{d\vec r}{dt}=(6.0t+2.0)\hat i+(4.0t+4.0)\hat j\ \mathrm{m/s}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç  
[math]\vec a=\frac{d\vec v}{dt}=6.0\hat i+4.0\hat j\ \mathrm{m/s^{2}}[/math].  
‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ì ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï: [math]|\vec a|=\sqrt{6^{2}+4^{2}}=\sqrt{52}=2\sqrt{13}\approx7.21\ \mathrm{m/s^{2}},\quad \theta=\tan^{-1}\!\left(\frac{4}{6}\right)=\tan^{-1}\!\left(\frac{2}{3}\right)\approx33.7^\circ[/math].

Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ò ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßÉ‡¶£ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤ [math]\nabla\cdot(\nabla\times \mathbf{F})=0[/math]‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø [math]\mathbf{F}=(P,Q,R)[/math] ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá

Question #83 (ID: 395609)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2019 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßá [math]\overrightarrow{A}=4 \widehat{i}+3 \widehat{j}+5 \hat{k}, \overrightarrow{B}=2 \hat{i}+\hat{j}+2 \widehat{k}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\overrightarrow{C}=x^{2} y \hat{i}+y^{2} z \hat{j}+z^{2} x \widehat{k}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ò. ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ [math]\overrightarrow{C}[/math] ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø? ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\overrightarrow{C}=x^{2} y \hat{i}+y^{2} z \hat{j}+z^{2} x \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{C}}=\overrightarrow{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{C}} \\ \hspace{1.5 cm} =\left|\begin{array}{ccc} \hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\ \dfrac{\partial}{\partial x} & \dfrac{\partial}{\partial y} & \dfrac{\partial}{\partial z} \\ x^{2} y & y^{2} z & z^{2} x \end{array}\right| \\ \hspace{1.5 cm}=\hat{i}\left\{\dfrac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(z^{2} x\right)-\dfrac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(y^{2} z\right)\right\} -\hat{j}\left\{\dfrac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(z^{2} x\right)-\dfrac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(x^{2} y\right)\right\} +\hat{k}\left\{\dfrac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(y^{2} z\right)-\dfrac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(x^{2} y\right)\right\} \\ \hspace{1.5 cm} =\hat{i}\left\{0-y^{2}\right\}-\hat{j}\left\{z^{2}-0\right\}+\hat{k}\left\{0-x^{2}\right\} \\ \hspace{1.5 cm} =-y^{2} \hat{i}-z^{2} \hat{j}-x^{2} \hat{k} \end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \therefore \operatorname{div}(\overrightarrow{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{C})=\overrightarrow{
abla} \cdot(\overrightarrow{
abla} \times \overrightarrow{C}) \\ \hspace{1.5 cm} =\left(\hat{i} \dfrac{\partial}{\partial x}+\hat{j} \dfrac{\partial}{\partial y}+\hat{\mathrm{k}} \dfrac{\partial}{\partial z}\right) \cdot\left(-y^{2} \hat{\mathrm{i}}-z^{2} \hat{\mathrm{j}}-\mathrm{x}^{2} \hat{\mathrm{k}}\right) \\ \hspace{1.5 cm}=-\left\{\dfrac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(y^{2}\right)+\dfrac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(z^{2}\right)+\dfrac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(x^{2}\right)\right\} \\ \hspace{1.5 cm} =-\{0+0+0\}=0 \end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶è‡¶¨, ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ [math]\overrightarrow{\rm{C}}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶™‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

Explanation:
‡¶ò ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Å ‚Äî ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶§‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ [math]\nabla\cdot(\nabla\times\mathbf{C})=0[/math]‡•§  
[math]\nabla\cdot(\nabla\times\mathbf{C})=\partial_x(\partial_y C_z-\partial_z C_y)+\partial_y(\partial_z C_x-\partial_x C_z)+\partial_z(\partial_x C_y-\partial_y C_x)=0[/math] ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶â‡ßé‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ó‡¶£ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ([math]\partial_x\partial_y=\partial_y\partial_x[/math]) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶π ‡¶™‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶Ü‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡•§

Question #84 (ID: 395599)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
y ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã x ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]y=5 x^{2}+6 x[/math]

Options:
‡¶ï. ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßÄ?
‡¶ñ. [math]\frac{d y}{d x}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶ì‡•§
‡¶ó. x = 5 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø x ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá y ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§
‡¶ò. ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ï‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶Æ ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡ß®‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ [math]\\[/math]
 ‡¶ñ [math]\frac{\mathrm{dy}}{\mathrm{dx}}[/math]
 ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá x ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßÅ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßÅ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø x ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá y ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ x ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá y ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§ [math]\\[/math]
 ‡¶ó‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, [math]y=5 x^{2}+6 x[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\mathrm{dy}}{\mathrm{dx}}=\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dx}}\left(5 \mathrm{x}^{2}+6 \mathrm{x}\right)=10 \mathrm{x}+6[/math]
 [math]x=5[/math]
 ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá,[math]\frac{\mathrm{dy}}{\mathrm{dx}}=10 \times 5+6=56 . \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 ‡¶ò‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá, [math]y=5 x^{2}+6 x[/math]
 .......(i)[math]\therefore[/math]
 (i) ‡¶®‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á,[math]\frac{d y}{d x}=\frac{d}{d x}\left(5 x^{2}+6 x\right)=10 x+6[/math]
 .......(ii)(ii) ‡¶®‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á,[math]\int(10 x+6 x) d x=5 x^{2}+6 x+c[/math]
 .......(iii)‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞, (i)-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£,[math]\begin{aligned}s=\int y d x & =\int\left(5 x^{2}+6 x\right) d x \\& =5 \int x^{2} d x+6 \int x d x\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 [math]s=5 \frac{x^{3}}{3}+6 \frac{x^{2}}{2}+c=\frac{5}{3} x^{3}+3 x^{2}+c[/math]
 .......(iv)(iv) ‡¶®‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á, [math]\frac{\mathrm{ds}}{\mathrm{dx}}=\frac{5}{3}\left(\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dx}} \mathrm{x}^{3}\right)+3\left(\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{dx}} \mathrm{x}^{2}\right)+0[/math]
 [math]=5 x^{2}+6 x[/math]
 .......(v)‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡•§

Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:
‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ï ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá; ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá y ‡¶π‡¶≤ x-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶ï‡•§  
‡¶ñ [math]\frac{dy}{dx}[/math] ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã y ‡¶è‡¶∞ x-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¢‡¶æ‡¶≤‡•§  
‡¶ó [math]y=5x^{2}+6x[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\frac{dy}{dx}=10x+6[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á x=5 ‡¶è [math]\frac{dy}{dx}=10\times5+6=56[/math]‡•§  
‡¶ò ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\frac{dy}{dx}=10x+6[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\int(10x+6)\,dx=5x^{2}+6x+C[/math], ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ y-‡¶ï‡ßá (‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ï ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ) ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‚Äî‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶è‡¶¨ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡•§

Question #85 (ID: 395600)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2022 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßá [math]\vec{A}=2 \hat{i}+2 \hat{j}-\hat{k}[/math], [math]\vec{B}=6 \hat{i}-3 \hat{j}+2 \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{c}}=\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}-\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}\right. -y) \hat{k} \text {. }[/math]

Options:
‡¶ò. ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá [math]\vec{C}[/math] ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò [math]\vec{C}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø [math]\operatorname{Curl} \vec{C}=0[/math]
 ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l} \vec{C}=\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}- \left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}\right. -y) \hat{k} \\ \vec{
abla}=\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k} \end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,[math]\begin{array}{l} \vec{
abla} \times \vec{C}= \\ =\left|\begin{array}{lll} \hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{\mathbf{k}} \\ \frac{\partial}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\ 6 x y+z^{3} & -3 x^{2}+z & 3 x z^{2}-y \end{array}\right| \\ =\hat{i}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(-3 x^{2}+z\right)\right\}+\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right)\right\}+\hat{k}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(-3 x^{2}+2 z\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(6 x y+z^{2}\right)\right\}\\ \begin{array}{l} =\{(0-1)-(1)\} \hat{i}+\left(3 z^{2}-3 z^{2}\right) \hat{j}+(-6 x-6 x) \hat{k} \\ =-2 \end{array} \end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ [math]\text { Curl } \vec{C}=\vec{
abla} \times \vec{C} 
eq 0 \therefore \vec{C}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ò ‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶≤ ‚Äî ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá
[math]\nabla\times\vec{C}=(\partial_y C_z-\partial_z C_y)\hat{i}+(\partial_z C_x-\partial_x C_z)\hat{j}+(\partial_x C_y-\partial_y C_x)\hat{k}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá
[math]\nabla\times\vec{C}=(-2)\hat{i}-12x\hat{k}\neq\vec{0},[/math]
‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶ï‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶® ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡ßü‡•§

Question #86 (ID: 395601)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2022 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ó ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßá, [math]Q=2 x y^{2} z^{3}-4 x y ~‡¶ì~ \vec{V}=\left(y^{2} \cos x+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+(2 y(\sin x-4) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}+2\right) \hat{k}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ò. ‡¶ê‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ê ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶® ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶ì‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ó V ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡•§‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, =(y¬≤cosx+z¬≥) √Æ + (2ysinx ‚Äì 4) ƒµ + (3xz¬≤ + 2) k‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤[math]\begin{aligned} \text { Curl } \overrightarrow{\mathbf{V}}=\vec{
abla} \times \vec{V}= & \left|\begin{array}{ccc} \hat{\mathrm{i}} & \hat{\mathrm{j}} & \hat{\mathbf{k}} \\ \frac{\partial}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\ y^{2} \cos x+z^{3} & 2 y \sin x-4 & 3 x z^{2}+2 \end{array}\right| \\ = & \hat{\mathrm{i}}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3 x z^{2}+2\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(2 y \sin x-4)\right\} -\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 x z^{2}+2\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(y^{2} \cos x+z^{3}\right)\right\} +\hat{k}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(2 y \sin x-4)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(y^{2} \cos x+z^{3}\right)\right\} \\ & =\hat{\mathrm{i}}(0-0)-\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left\{3 z^{2}-3 z^{2}\right\}+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\{2 y \cos x-2 y \cos x\} \\ & =0 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+0 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+0 \hat{\mathrm{k}}=0\end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ [math]\vec{
abla} \times \vec{V}=0[/math]
, ‡¶è‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø [math]\vec{V}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ê ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ê ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶® ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
[math]\nabla\times\vec{V}=\begin{vmatrix}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\ \partial_x & \partial_y & \partial_z \\ y^{2}\cos x+z^{3} & 2y(\sin x-4) & 3xz^{2}+2 \end{vmatrix}[/math]  
[math](\nabla\times\vec{V})_{i}=\partial_{y}(3xz^{2}+2)-\partial_{z}(2y(\sin x-4))=0-0=0[/math]  
[math](\nabla\times\vec{V})_{j}=\partial_{z}(y^{2}\cos x+z^{3})-\partial_{x}(3xz^{2}+2)=3z^{2}-3z^{2}=0[/math]  
[math](\nabla\times\vec{V})_{k}=\partial_{x}(2y(\sin x-4))-\partial_{y}(y^{2}\cos x+z^{3})=2y\cos x-2y\cos x=0[/math]  
‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶è‡¶¨ [math]\nabla\times\vec{V}=0[/math], ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶® ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á (‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶®/irrotational)‡•§

Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2022 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board

Question:
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ó ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßá, [math]Q=2 x y^{2} z^{3}-4 x y ~‡¶ì~ \vec{V}=\left(y^{2} \cos x+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+(2 y(\sin x-4) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}+2\right) \hat{k}[/math]

Options:
‡¶ó. (1, ‚àí1, 2) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ê ‡¶Ö‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞, [math]Q=2 x y^{2} z^{3}-4 x y[/math]
‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü,[math]\begin{array}{l}\operatorname{grad\theta }=\vec{
abla} \mathrm{Q} \\ =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}} \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{z}} \hat{\mathrm{k}}\right) \mathrm{Q} \\ =\left(\frac{\partial \theta}{\partial \mathrm{i}} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\frac{\partial \mathrm{Q}}{\partial \mathrm{j}}+\frac{\partial \mathrm{Q}}{\partial \mathrm{z}} \hat{\mathrm{k}}\right)\\ =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(2 x y^{2} z^{3}-4 x y\right) \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(2 x y^{2} z^{3}-4 x y\right) \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2 x y^{2} z^{3}-4 x y\right) \hat{k}\right)\\ =\left(2 y^{2} z^{3}-4 y\right) \hat{i}+\left(4 x y z^{3}-4 x\right) \hat{j}+6 x y^{2} z^{2} \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® [math](1,-1,2)[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá[math]\begin{array}{l} \vec{
abla} \mathrm{Q}=\left\{2 \cdot(-1)^{2} \cdot 2^{3}-4(-1)\right\} \hat{\mathrm{i}} +\left\{4 \cdot 1 \cdot(-1) \cdot(2)^{3}-4 \cdot 1\right\} \hat{\mathrm{j}}+6 \cdot 1(-1)^{2} \cdot\left(2^{2}\right) \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ =20 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-36 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+24 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:
‡¶ó ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶â‡ßé‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞: [math]\nabla Q=\Big(\frac{\partial Q}{\partial x},\frac{\partial Q}{\partial y},\frac{\partial Q}{\partial z}\Big)[/math]. ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\frac{\partial Q}{\partial x}=2y^{2}z^{3}-4y,\;\frac{\partial Q}{\partial y}=4xyz^{3}-4x,\;\frac{\partial Q}{\partial z}=6xy^{2}z^{2}[/math]; ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ [math](1,-1,2)[/math]-‡¶è ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla Q(1,-1,2)=(20,-36,24)=20\hat{i}-36\hat{j}+24\hat{k}[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡¶§‡•§

Question #88 (ID: 395603)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p(x, y, z)=2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z[/math] ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{A}=(2 x+y) \hat{i} +\left(3 y+z^{2}\right) \hat{j}+(-5 z+x) \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{B}=(6 x y+ \left.z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat {k}[/math] ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡•§

Options:
‡¶ó. (2,‚àí 1, ‚àí2) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá p ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]p(x, y, z)=2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{A}=(2 x+y) \hat{i} +\left(3 y+z^{2}\right) \hat{j}+(-5 z+x) \hat{k}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{B}=(6 x y+ \left.z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat{k}[/math]
 ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡•§‡¶ó. (2,‚àí 1, ‚àí2) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá p ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§

Explanation:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]p(x, y, z) =2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z[/math]
p ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü[math]\begin{array}{l} \operatorname{grad} \mathrm{p}=\vec{\nabla} \mathrm{p} \\ =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{x}} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{y}} \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{z}} \hat{\mathrm{k}}\right) \mathrm{p} \\ =\frac{\partial \mathrm{p}}{\partial \mathrm{i}} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\frac{\partial \mathrm{p}}{\partial \mathrm{j}} \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\frac{\partial \mathrm{p}}{\partial \mathrm{z}} \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ =\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z\right) \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z\right) \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z\right) \hat{k}\\ =\left(2 y^{4}-2 x z\right) \hat{i}+\left(8 x y^{3}\right) \hat{j}-x^{2} \hat{k} \end{array}[/math]
(2, -1, -2) ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá p ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü[math]\begin{array}{l} =\left\{2(-1)^{4}-2.2(-2)\right\} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\left\{8.2(-1)^{3}\right\} \hat{\mathrm{j}}-\left\{(2)^{2}\right\} \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ =10 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-16 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-4 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \text { (Ans.) } \end{array}[/math]

Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p(x, y, z)=2 x y^{4}-x^{2} z[/math] ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{A}=(2 x+y) \hat{i} +\left(3 y+z^{2}\right) \hat{j}+(-5 z+x) \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{B}=(6 x y+ \left.z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡•§

Options:
‡¶ò. ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§ [math]\overrightarrow{\mathbf{A}}[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\overrightarrow{\mathbf{B}}[/math] ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, [math]\vec{A}=(2 x+y) \hat{i}+\left(3 y+z^{2}\right) \hat{j}+(-5 z+x) \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ [math]\operatorname{div} \vec{A}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} =\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{A} \\ =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left\{(2 x+y) \hat{i}+\left(3 y+z^{2}\right) \hat{j}+(-5 z+x) \hat{k}\right\} \\ =\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(2 x+y)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3 y+z^{2}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}(-5 z+x) \\ =2+{3}-5=0 \end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{A}=0[/math]
 ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßü‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤‡•§[math]\vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤[math]\operatorname{curl} \vec{A}=\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A} =\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\ \frac{\partial}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\ 2 x+y & 3 y+z^{2} & -5 z+x \end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\qquad \begin{array}{l} =\hat{i}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(-5 z+x)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(3 y+z^{2}\right)\right\}-\hat{j}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}(-5 z+x)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(2 x+y^{2}\right)\right\} \\ +\hat{k}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 y+z^{2}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}(2 x+y)\right. \\ =\hat{\mathrm{i}}\{0-2 \mathrm{z}\}-\hat{\mathrm{j}}\{1-0\}+\hat{\mathrm{k}}\{0-1\} \\ =-2 z \hat{i}-\hat{j}-\hat{k} \\ \end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ [math]\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A} 
eq \overrightarrow{0}[/math]
 ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞, [math]\vec{B}=\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\vec{B}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ [math]\operatorname{div} \vec{B}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} =\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{B} \\ =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left\{\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat{k}\right\} \\ =\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3 x^{2}-z\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \\ =6 y+0+6 x z \\ =6 x z+6 y \end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{B} 
eq 0[/math]
 ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec{b}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßü‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§[math]\vec{B}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ [math]\text { curl } \overrightarrow{\mathbf{B}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} =\vec{
abla} \times \vec{B} \\ =\left|\begin{array}{ccc} \hat{\mathbf{i}} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\ \frac{\partial}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\ 6 x y+z^{3} & 3 x^{2}-z & 3 x z^{2}-y \end{array}\right| \\ =\hat{i}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(3 x^{2}-z\right)\right\} \\ -\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial \dot{x}}\left(3 x z^{2}-\mathrm{y}\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial \mathrm{z}}\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right)\right\}+\hat{\mathrm{k}} \text {. } \\ \left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 x^{2}-z\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right)\right\} \\ =\hat{\mathrm{i}}(-1+1)-\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(3 z^{2}-3 z^{2}\right)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}(6 x-6 x) \\ =0 \hat{i}-0 \hat{j}+0 \hat{k} \\ =0 \\\end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§

Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ò [math]\nabla\cdot\vec A=\partial_x(2x+y)+\partial_y(3y+z^2)+\partial_z(-5z+x)=2+3-5=0[/math] ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec A[/math] ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ [math]\nabla\times\vec A=(\partial_yA_z-\partial_zA_y,\partial_zA_x-\partial_xA_z,\partial_xA_y-\partial_yA_x)=(-2z,-1,-1)\ne\vec0[/math] ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
[math]\nabla\cdot\vec B=\partial_x(6xy+z^3)+\partial_y(3x^2-z)+\partial_z(3xz^2-y)=6y+6xz\ne0[/math] ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec B[/math] ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\nabla\times\vec B=(\partial_yB_z-\partial_zB_y,\partial_zB_x-\partial_xB_z,\partial_xB_y-\partial_yB_x)=(0,0,0)[/math] ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø, ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á, [math]\vec{A}[/math]

‡¶ò‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, 1‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞[math]\vec{A}=\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat{k}[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø, ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶ê ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶ê ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§[math]\vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏[math]\begin{array}{l}\operatorname{div} \vec{A}=\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{A} \\ =\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{j}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot\left\{\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right) \hat{i}+\left(3 x^{2}-z\right) \hat{j}+\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \hat{k}\right\} \\ =\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3 x^{2}-z\right)+\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right) \\ =6 y+6 x z 
eq 0 \end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ, [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{A} 
eq 0[/math]
, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞, [math]\vec{a}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤[math]\begin{array}{l} \text { Curl } \vec{A}=\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A}\\ =\left|\begin{array}{ccc} \hat{\mathrm{i}} & \hat{\mathrm{j}} & \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ \frac{\partial}{\partial x} & \frac{\partial}{\partial y} & \frac{\partial}{\partial z} \\ 6 x y+z^{3} & 3 x^{2}-z & 3 x z^{2}-y \end{array}\right| \\ =\hat{\mathrm{i}}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(3 \dot{x}^{2}-z\right)\right\}-\hat{j}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 x z^{2}-y\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial z}\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right)\right\} \\ +\hat{k}\left\{\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left(3 x^{2}-z\right)-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left(6 x y+z^{3}\right)\right\} \\ =\hat{\mathrm{i}}(-1+1)-\hat{\mathrm{j}}\left(3 z^{2}-3 z^{2}\right)+\hat{k}(6 x-6 x) \\ =0 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-0 \hat{j}+0 \hat{k} \\ =0 \end{array}[/math]
‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá, [math]\vec{
abla} \times \vec{A}=0[/math]
, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé [math]\vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶ò‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§

Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\nabla\cdot\vec{A}=\partial_x(6xy+z^3)+\partial_y(3x^2-z)+\partial_z(3xz^2-y)=6y+0+6xz=6(y+xz)[/math] ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶∂‡ßÇ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º [math]\nabla\times\vec{A}=(\partial_y A_z-\partial_z A_y)\hat{i}+(\partial_z A_x-\partial_x A_z)\hat{j}+(\partial_x A_y-\partial_y A_x)\hat{k}=0[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞ [math]\mathbb{R}^3[/math]-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§

Question:
‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ [math]\overrightarrow{\mathbf{E}}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ê ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathbf{E}}[/math] ‡¶ï‡¶§?

Options:


Correct Answer: ‡¶ñ

Solution:
[math]\vec{E}=x \hat{i}+y \hat{j}+z \hat{k}[/math]
 [math]\vec{
abla} \cdot \vec{E}=\left(\frac{\partial}{\partial x} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial y} \hat{i}+\frac{\partial}{\partial z} \hat{k}\right) \cdot(x \hat{i}+y \hat{i}+z \hat{k})=\frac{\partial x}{\partial x}+\frac{\partial y}{\partial y}+\frac{\partial z}{\partial z}[/math]
 [math]=(1+1+1)=3[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá [math]\overrightarrow{\mathbf{E}}=(x,y,z)[/math] ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{\nabla}\cdot\overrightarrow{\mathbf{E}}=\frac{\partial x}{\partial x}+\frac{\partial y}{\partial y}+\frac{\partial z}{\partial z}=1+1+1=3[/math].
